Important Foreign Telegrams II

Picard Undertakes Another High-Altitude Exploration 52

Ascends by Balloon to a Height of 16,500 Meters

Sends Wireless Reports of High-Altitude News from the Stratosphere

▲ A Reuters telegram from Bern, Switzerland, on the 18th stated that the first wireless telegram from the stratosphere was received on Earth. This telegram was sent by Professor Picard, who reported that the balloon had risen more than ten miles, exceeding his own previous record. The balloon is still rising slowly.

▲ A Reuters telegram from Zurich on the 18th stated that Professor Picard and his assistant Dr. Kossins made their second attempt to reach the stratosphere at 5:05 this morning. Picard and Kossins were seated in an airtight aluminum chamber, which was attached to a large balloon. Last night, Picard saw that the weather was turning better, so he re-examined the aluminum chamber and the various sophisticated instruments it contained, including a wireless transmitter. Then he made gas to fill the balloon. A large crowd came to watch, all wanting to see Picard rise into the sky. After working busily all night, they took off after dawn, rising slowly. This trip is intended to capture images of cosmic rays and obtain their theoretical basis. According to reports, Picard and Kipfer rode a balloon together on May 27th of last year in Würzburg, Bavaria, and entered the stratosphere. At that time, there was an anticyclone, and the balloon drifted in the air for 18 hours before falling somewhere 160 kilometers south. This trip reached a height of about 15 and a half kilometers above the ground, approximately four kilometers into the stratosphere, breaking the record for the altitude reached by a manned balloon or airplane.

▲ A National News Agency telegram from Zurich on the 18th stated that Professor Picard of the Free University of Brussels rose in a balloon from the Dübendorf airfield here at 5:05 this morning to conduct his second high-altitude test of the stratosphere. The main purpose of this trip is to continue studying cosmic rays and calibrate the various records obtained during the first ascent last May. The round chamber in which Picard and his assistant Gilboe were riding has been greatly improved compared to last year. The chamber is made of an alloy of lead and is completely coated with white enamel to reflect sunlight and prevent the interior from being as hot as it was last year. The observation windows have also increased from one to eight, plus an entrance. The arrangement of the window holes allows people in the chamber to fully see the atmospheric phenomena around the balloon above and the ground below. The entrance and exit have also been greatly improved. If opened during flight, they can be closed from the inside, and all equipment is impermeable to water to prevent the airship from unfortunately falling into the sea or lakes when it lands. Even the balloon piston door that enters the chamber passes through a mercury chamber to prevent water seepage. The diameter of the chamber is 2.2 meters and weighs about 550 pounds. In addition to various scientific instruments and two seats, there is also a shortwave wireless transceiver. The balloon's bag is the largest in the world, with a capacity of 14,000 cubic meters. Its load, including the ballast lead, is 3,520 pounds. Before departing, Picard told people that he had planned a third ascent, the location of which is planned to be in North America or near Hudson Bay, because it is closest to the Earth's magnetic pole. Although this move is costly, it has immeasurable value for studying the aurora borealis and other sky phenomena. He also said that the ballast lead he carried this time weighed 1,650 kilograms. As for whether the balloon will go north or south after rising, it is difficult to predict. After the balloon was unmoored and rose slowly, Picard waved goodbye to thousands of spectators from the window and gave a flying kiss to his wife and family. Also, when the balloon was unmoored, Swiss aviator Mittelholzer drove a three-motor Fokker airplane and carried a film camera to set off first, intending to fly with the balloon to 5,000 meters to shoot a film, but returned to the airfield after 20 minutes, saying that the balloon was rising extremely fast and had reached 4,900 meters. After that, the ascent accelerated even more, so he stopped chasing it. Later, at 7:45, Picard's balloon floated past Richterschwanden, and at about 7:30, it flew past Wallenstadt, close to the Austrian border. According to electrical measurements, its altitude reached 15,000 meters. Continuing telegram: Professor Picard has reached the highest altitude ever reached by humans, far higher than his last time. At 11:15 this morning, his balloon passed over the sky of Reichenau-Garten, about 100 miles southeast of Zurich. At that time, he was heading towards Urdorf on the border between Switzerland and Austria. Its altitude was between 17,000 meters and 18,000 meters above the ground. According to the last ascent, it reached 51,793 feet, which is about 15,000 meters.

▲ A Havas news agency telegram from Milan, Italy, on the 18th stated that Professor Picard's balloon has descended near the village of Iseo, near Brescia, Italy.

▲ A Havas news agency telegram from Mirik, Switzerland, on the 18th stated that Professor Picard set off this morning and ascended with his assistant Kossin for high-altitude exploration. This exploration has aroused great interest in scientific circles in various countries, because Picard's ascent may be able to observe the cosmic rays discovered by Professor Millikan of the United States in the high altitude. This morning, the airfield was obscured by dense fog. After the rope holding the balloon to the ground broke, the balloon rose. The initial ascent was very slow, but after Picard and Kossin took their seats at the bottom of the balloon, the balloon ascended in an accelerated state. When it rose to a height of 1,500 meters, the balloon moved south. At 8:00 AM, the Santis Observatory reported that the balloon was flying over the Baniña mountain range at a height of 11 to 12 kilometers. The balloon was still rising rapidly. At 10:40, the Davos reported that the balloon was still moving south and could no longer be seen with the naked eye. At 11:30, Professor Picard sent a wireless message saying, "Flying over the Engadine mountain range at a height of 16,500 meters. Everything is going well, but it is extremely cold." At 11:40, a second report was received, saying, "To avoid falling into the Adriatic Sea, we are landing. We can now see Lake Garda."

▲ A Havas news agency telegram from Vienna on the 18th stated that the Austrian people have paid close attention to Professor Picard's high-altitude exploration. When Picard's airship appeared in the sky over Voralberg, the director of the Aspern airfield in Vienna immediately notified meteorologically skilled aviators to exchange messages with Professor Picard by wireless and transmit reports to the Austrian Aviation Association at any time. The National Radio Station constantly communicated with Picard and broadcast news to various places when the balloon arrived in Vienna.

Soviet Union's Autumn Planting Plan for This Year 63

▲ Moscow (TASS, 17th) – According to the plan approved by the People's Commissariat of Agriculture, the Soviet Union's autumn planting this year will cover 42,000,000 hectares, of which 29,000,000 hectares will be operated by collective farms, 9,000,000 hectares by individual farms, and 3,500,000 hectares by state-owned farms. The harvest period for industrial grains is approaching, and harvesting has already begun in several places. The area sown with industrial grains this year has increased by 1,000,000 hectares compared to last year. 500,000 hectares, or 20 percent, of hemp fields were harvested by August 10th. This year's cotton harvest is slightly earlier than last year. Currently, 80 percent of cotton fields, 50 percent of hemp fields, and 60 percent of sugar beet fields have been collectivized. 800 state-owned machinery stations are assisting with the cultivation of industrial grains, and 60 percent of the cotton harvest has been mechanized.

Zhu Jiqing's Three Declarations 66

Zhu Jiqing, Commander-in-Chief of the Northeastern National Salvation Army, recently issued three declarations, which are recorded as follows:

▲ A Letter to Compatriots in Cities and Villages of Northeast China: This time, the Japanese invasion and occupation of the three northeastern provinces is a major event related to the survival of the Chinese nation. All compatriots across the country, unwilling to be slaves of a conquered nation, should make a common determination, regardless of regional differences, to face the national crisis. Recently, young people from all walks of life in the mainland have been continuously coming to the northeast to join the volunteer army, and donations of military supplies have also been extremely enthusiastic. All this proves that resisting the Japanese invaders has now become a unified trend throughout the country. The Northeast, at present, is completely under the trampling of the Japanese invaders. From September 18th of last year to now, it has been almost a year. The fire is getting hotter, and the water is getting deeper. Local compatriots feel the pain to the bone, and their awareness of foreign matters is naturally more profound and clear than that of compatriots in the mainland. Then, is it not a divinely ordained responsibility to unite and resist the Japanese invaders to the end until all lost land is recovered? Since invading the Northeast, the Japanese invaders have inflicted all kinds of cruel oppression on Chinese compatriots, and the following matters are particularly hateful: (1) Confiscation of Firearms: Civilian firearms are essential for self-defense. After confiscation, the power of self-defense is completely lost. In the future, no matter how rampant the Japanese and their ignorant military police are, there will be no possibility of resistance. Japan had previously implemented this law in Korea. Not only firearms, but also ordinary kitchen knives used by Koreans are subject to strict restrictions. To this day, 20 million Koreans are swallowing their voices and enduring beatings, with no hope of recovery. This is truly a lesson from the past. (2) Reclamation of Banner Lands: The lands of the various banners in the Northeast have long been opened up, especially the banner lands throughout Liaoning, which have long been occupied and managed by Han people at a price, and they have lived in harmony. This time, the Japanese invaders actually used the puppet state to fabricate excuses to reclaim them. In general, the most poisonous method for foreigners to control colonies is to cut off the economic lifeline of the local people. The intention of the Japanese invaders is truly a matter that everyone knows. Once implemented, the precious land on which countless compatriots depend for their livelihoods will be plundered, and they will have to become proletarians and live a miserable life. Originally, the number of so-called banner people currently existing in the eastern provinces is limited. The land reclaimed by the puppet state will be enjoyed by the banner people in name only. In fact, very few will benefit. Many fertile lands will only be freely used by the Japanese and some Koreans who are willing to be dogs. (3) Strict Implementation of Informing: Resisting the Japanese invaders is what everyone naturally thinks. Precisely because of this, the more the Japanese invaders suspect, the more restrictive methods emerge endlessly. The inspection of travelers, the search of homes, and the harassment are too numerous to mention. The use of Chinese traitors to allow informing is especially alarming. Among our compatriots, there are indeed those who participate in anti-Japanese work or join volunteer army organizations and are arrested because they are informed. There is nothing to regret about this. But among them, there are many cowardly compatriots who are afraid of the fierce power and are cautious in their actions. They have no actions at all, but because of the revenge of enemies and private grudges, or because the extortion of thugs has not been successful, they are also falsely accused and wronged because of informing, and their lives and property are sacrificed. How painful and hateful this is! In addition to these various atrocities, they are too numerous to mention, regardless of urban or rural areas. Compatriots in the countryside are generous and passionate, resisting the Japanese invaders, cutting off their blood and righteousness, and their loyalty reaches the sky. Compatriots in the cities, due to different circumstances, have a slightly slower resistance performance, but the anti-Japanese enthusiasm in everyone's heart has never been less intense. This is conceivable. However, I still have some concerns. Although both urban and rural areas suffer from the disasters of the Japanese invaders, the degree is quite different. Generally speaking, compatriots in the cities are more easily protected because there have always been more troops and police stationed locally. The number of self-defense firearms purchased is small, and their main occupation is in business, and there is not much agriculture, so the two points of the Japanese invaders' confiscation of firearms and reclamation of banner lands have little impact on compatriots in the cities. As for the various personnel of the Japanese invaders, they are mostly stationed in urban areas, and it is easier for compatriots in the cities to contact them. The informers have some scruples, so they are naturally less harmed than compatriots in the countryside. Moreover, the Japanese are very cunning. At this time, the entire territory of the Northeast is disturbed and uneasy, and it is inconvenient to make enemies everywhere. It is a very good strategy to feign appeasement and win over the hearts of the people for a part of the people in the urban areas. In the past, at the beginning of the Japanese conquest of Korea, they also suppressed the countryside and relaxed the urban areas. At that time, the resistance of the Korean people was also fierce in the countryside and slow in the urban areas. Later, the eight-province cleanup policy changed, and the treatment of the people in the urban areas was a hundred times worse than in the countryside. Those with a little wealth and knowledge were all labeled as reactionaries and arbitrarily arrested and killed without any politeness. The heavy taxes and miscellaneous taxes were as dense as the hair of an ox, and they were mostly borne by the people in the cities. The people in the urban areas regretted this later, but it was too late. Now the Japanese invaders are still using the method of deceiving the Korean people to deceive the compatriots in the urban areas of the Northeast. If the compatriots in the urban areas do not have a very distant vision and follow the Japanese invaders' cunning plans, then the disasters suffered by the people in the urban areas of Korea will be seen again in the Northeast. This is something that cannot but be worried about. Therefore, I would like to earnestly and sincerely advise compatriots from all walks of life in both urban and rural areas, especially those in the cities. Urban and rural areas are one body. The city is like the head of a person, and the countryside is like the limbs of a person. It is impossible for the limbs to be destroyed and the head to be healthy. From now on, everyone should be thoroughly aware of this, be of one mind and one heart, and work together to drive the Japanese invaders out of the country in order to protect the reputation of the Chinese nation and avoid the re-enactment of the Korean tragedy. I am not talented, and I will secretly pray for it. (To be continued)

The Course of Suppressing Bandits in Eastern Hubei 68

▲ Important Passes in Northeastern Hubei Are Recovered One by One

A communication from Hankou states that eastern Hubei is where the main force of the Red Army is located, with the 10th, 11th, 12th, 13th, 73rd, and Independent First Divisions, along with the Red Guards, claiming to have more than 50,000 people. Their lairs are in Qiliping, Huang'an, and other places, with Hekou Town, Lvwangcheng, and Huangpi Station as their forward bases. They attempted to cut off the southern section of the Pinghan Railway with a small number of troops, while the majority would occupy Macheng, Songbu, and Huangpi to advance on Wuhan. The bloody battle of Huangpi in early January, the long siege of Macheng in July, and the repeated destruction of the Pinghan Railway were all carried out according to this plan. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek therefore adopted an effective steady approach, using the 30th and 31st Divisions of Zhang Yinxiang's army and the division of Hao Mengling to firmly defend the area from Macheng to Huangpi. He also deployed heavy troops from Chen Jicheng and Wei Lihuang on the east side of the Pinghan Railway, forming an arc-shaped encirclement line against the bandits in the Huang'an and Qiliping areas. Once the deployment was complete, the general offensive began on the 9th of this month. At that time, Liu Zhi, the Pacification Director stationed in Henan, sent troops from Zhang Fang and Ma Hongkui to attack and advance towards Bopi River, Dongxin Township, and Shuangchang Township, successively occupying various places and posing a major threat to the Red bandits. On the first day of the general offensive, Chen Jicheng's troops advanced south from Xuanhuadian, and Wei Lihuang's troops advanced from the original Chen location to Cai Town, Xia Town, and Changxingling, bandit gangs occupying Hekou Town Huangpi Station were panicked to see the national army advancing step by step. Wei and Chen's troops launched a fierce attack on the second day. Wei's troops divided into three routes, one via Yaojiaji, one via Liujiaji, Si Gu Dun, and one via Cai Town, advancing towards Hekou Town. The bandits were besieged on three sides and collapsed one after another. In this battle, more than 3,000 bandits were killed and even more were captured. During the fierce battle, the bandits hiding in the northeast team of Hekou Town hoped to come to support. The government troops took advantage of their unpreparedness and launched a pincer attack, almost annihilating the bandits. The remaining bandits fled back to Huang'an and continued to make a final struggle in the area from Liangtinggang to Dongyuemiao. Wei's troops occupied Hekou Town and pursued the victory. On the afternoon of the 12th, they separately occupied all the highlands in the areas of Luojiazai, Liangtingguan, Banbiandian, and Hongdian outside Huang'an city. On the morning of the 13th, the troops worked together to attack the city. The city hills and important passes were successively destroyed by artillery fire. The bandits had no will to fight due to excessive casualties. The various armies still attacked bravely. At 2 p.m., the north gate was broken by Li Mo'an's division of Wei's troops. For a time, the order in the city was in chaos, and the remaining bandits fled out of the city in embarrassment and retreated to the northeast. In this battle, thousands of bandits were captured and countless military supplies were seized. When Wei's troops besieged Huang'an, Chen Jicheng's troops successively occupied Huangpi Station, Lvwangcheng, Huajiahe, Tushahe, Guojia Xin Township and other places, encircling and suppressing the bandit lairs in Qiliping. After Huang'an was captured, morale was boosted. On the 13th, Chen's troops made contact with the bandits. After a fierce battle that lasted for a day and night, the Red bandits suffered extremely heavy losses. On the 14th, Li Yutang's division of Chen's troops was the first to attack the bandit lair in Qiliping. The remaining bandits hid in the northeastern highlands. Chen's troops are currently searching and will be able to resolve the situation within days. Huang'an, Qiliping, and Hekou Town are all important areas in northeastern Hubei. They fell into the hands of the bandits for eight months. The defensive works were arranged very strictly. This time, the government troops attacked and successively recovered them in just a few days. Tens of thousands of bandits collapsed in an instant, which was truly unexpected. After receiving the report, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek immediately sent a telegram to the various armies, encouraging them to continue to fight and stating that the Red bandits were definitely not a strong enemy and that they could defeat the many with the few and win more with less. The original telegram briefly stated that this time, in the recovery of Huang'an, our Sixth Column broke the definite report of tens of thousands of troops in front of us. It was the 10th, 11th, 12th, 13th, 14th and other divisions of the bandits, as well as the First Independent Division, and an unidentified division, a total of seven divisions, as well as the Red Guards, independent regiments, battalions, etc., totaling no less than 60,000 people. Their 11th Division, known as the Iron Army, has been almost completely wiped out by us. A total of more than 18,000 bandits were killed or wounded. At that time, the puppet government forced the Huang'an County town to send two able-bodied men from each household to carry the dead and wounded. Now, north and south of Dongyuemiao, as far as Huang'an County, corpses are still lying everywhere. This shows that the bandits are definitely not a strong enemy. As long as we can fight, we can defeat the many with the few and win more with less. I hope that everyone will work hard to completely eliminate the ugly creatures and achieve complete success, etc. The post-disaster relief in Huang'an needs to be organized urgently. The fellow villagers association of the county has specially presented it to the Pacification Office, requesting a huge amount of money to be allocated for immediate relief. The original presentation described the sufferings of the people of Huang'an, which were unbearable to hear, and is recorded as follows: "Your county, Huang'an, has been ravaged by the Communist bandits since the 16th year of the Republic of China. The authorities have repeatedly sent troops to suppress them, but the bandit forces have become more and more rampant day by day, and they have finally grown in size. The county seat has fallen into the bandit lair, and the four townships have become red zones. The rural economy has been completely destroyed, and social ethics have been completely destroyed. The old and weak have been poisoned by them, and the strong have been sacrificed by them. Farm implements have been cast into spears and halberds, and cattle have been used as food. Even the thatched huts have been reduced to ashes. The beautiful fields have been reduced to overgrown weeds. The remains of the dead are abandoned in barren hills, and the survivors have moved away and are lingering. The wilderness is desolate, and the sound of chickens and dogs cannot be heard. The thousands of villages are dim, and only the traces of rats and foxes remain. The severity of the disaster is not only the crown of our Hubei, but also an unprecedented catastrophe and a tragedy that the world has never experienced. Now that the large army is encircling and suppressing them, the bandit disaster will be quelled in a matter of days. However, in the recovered area, there is no grain left, and the source of life has been cut off. If we do not urgently raise a huge amount of money to provide relief on the ground, what will the children and grandchildren be entrusted to? We have always relied on Your Excellency to be concerned about our sufferings, to care about our hunger and drowning, and to have special pity for these refugees. We respectfully request that you quickly allocate a huge amount of money to provide timely relief, to cleanse the wounds on the people's bodies, and to enable them to ascend to the spring terrace and the summer house together. We also request that you select and dispatch competent personnel to distribute the money quickly. We sincerely beg for your mercy and await your orders with trepidation." (August 16th)

The Sixth Day of the Continued Trial of the Noulens Case (Continued) 69

▲ Noulens Roars in Court and is Ordered to Leave the Court

▲ The Prosecutor Reports on the Progress of the Case

▲ The Debate Ends and the Verdict is Scheduled for the 19th

At the same time, a note written in French was found on the desk, meaning "I will come again at 2:30 this afternoon." So, the Western police waited in the room. At that time, a woman, namely Wang Deli, used a key to open the door from the outside and came in. When she saw two strangers, she said that she had come to the wrong place and asked if she knew Noulens. She did not answer. A receipt was found in her handbag, knowing that she lived at No. 745 Huayuan Road, Hongkou. The Western police went there to search, and found a clue from a garden entrance ticket, and cracked the case at No. 66 Hede Road, where many bank savings books were found, totaling 47,000 yuan deposited in various banks, all in the names of Chinese people. At the same time, Chinese and Western seals were also found to withdraw the deposits. This deposit was used by Noulens to direct the Red Army in various places, but this is only part of it. Based on the documents and deposits found, it is determined that Noulens' purpose in harming the Republic of China also has the following proofs: (1) A person who looks after the house and a rent collector have proved in the High Court that Noulens is the guest living in Room 30, Block C, No. 49 Nanjing Road. (2) Since Noulens knew that there was U.S. dollars in the steel box, the documents in the steel box must be Noulens'. (3) The handwriting of Noulens' letter to the Meifeng Bank has been identified by the appraiser of the police station as being consistent with the other two documents. (4) Xiang Zhongfa, the leader of the Communist bandits, once confessed that the Far East Director of the Third International was Noulens, also known as Lao Maozi and Ainase, which shows that these are all his aliases. Even if Ainase is another person, why doesn't Noulens point it out? (5) Noulens said that he was a teacher in Shanghai. How could a teacher have so much money, and why would he have wireless registration in four places and eight post office boxes? (6) The Far East Director includes Japan, Annam, Saigon, and other parts. The scope is even larger than the Chinese Director. The purpose is to instigate farmers and workers to organize the Red Army, provide funds, and destroy our country's political organization. Based on the above points, there is no doubt that he has committed the crime of harming the Republic of China. As for Wang Deli, a document typed in English with handwritten additions was also found. The handwriting is the same as the handwriting left in Room 30, Block C, No. 49 Nanjing Road. Her purpose is the same as Noulens'. Regardless of whether they are husband and wife, she and Noulens have the same purpose. Xiang Zhongfa once confessed that Noulens' wife is very powerful, but they are not really husband and wife. They were sent by the Third International to monitor Noulens' work. If Wang had no close relationship with Noulens, why would so many important documents in Noulens' room not be kept secret from her, and why would she be allowed to enter and leave freely, and why would she have the same key? When Wang was arrested, she stated that she had gone to the wrong place and did not know Noulens. Why does she now say that they are husband and wife? By analogy, it can be seen that her work is Noulens' work, and there is no doubt that she is an accomplice. Therefore, she should be prosecuted together in accordance with Articles 1, 2, 5, and 6 of the Emergency Law for the Punishment of Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. However, whether the amnesty case regulations should be applied to reduce her sentence should be decided by the presiding judge. After the prosecutor's argument was completed, the presiding judge asked the lawyer Chen Ying if there was a debate. Chen replied that before the evidence is fully verified, the order is first the prosecutor's argument, then the defendant's statement, and then the lawyer's defense. Now the defendant has not yet made a statement, and the elected lawyer has not obtained the defendant's opinion, so he cannot defend immediately. (Question) The defendant is making a lot of noise in court today, so according to Article 61 of the Court Organization Law, he is ordered to leave the court because the defendant is not obeying the order. (Answer) The lawyer declares doubt about Article 299 of the Criminal Procedure Law and asks for a ruling first. (Question) This court has the right to order him to leave the court for violating Articles 61 and 62 of the Court Organization Law and violating the order, and according to Article 63, no appeal is allowed. (Answer) Now the lawyer is ordered to defend. Please ask whether the order is based on the qualification of election or designation. (Question) Noulens asked you to defend him, and today he added a signature to your letter of commission in court, so of course it is the qualification of election. (Answer) The defendant is accused of endangering the Republic of China, a crime punishable by death. If there is any doubt, please ask the presiding judge to rule on the necessity first.

Westward Journey (II) 70

▲Shaanxi Only Lacks a Little Water

After a sudden clearing of heavy rain, a constant cool breeze blew, and the pleasure we felt greatly increased our spirit to move forward. On the afternoon of the 11th, at 5:00 PM, everyone hurriedly packed their luggage and handed it over to the Longhai Railway authorities, asking porters to load it onto the train. After a boisterous half-hour, we split up into rickshaws, racing each other straight to the station.

We are ashamed—we are truly very ashamed, because we have unconsciously become slightly tainted with the colors of the aristocracy and the spirit of imperialism. When we arrived at the station, there were already many people holding flags filled with various slogans, coming to see us off. After I boarded the train, I learned that this was a special train prepared for us by the Longhai Railway, and the decorations and furnishings were very beautiful and comfortable. After the train departed at 6:15 PM, we arrived at Sishui at 7:47 PM that evening, Luoyang at 10:21 PM, Xin'an at 11:43 PM, Mianchi at 1:40 AM in the middle of the night, Guanyintang at 2:37 AM, and Shanzhou at 4:36 AM. On the 12th, at 5:46 AM at dawn, we arrived at Lingbao, and Tongguan at 9:47 AM. Along the way, at each station, there were armed comrades with unusually neat uniforms, saluting us and putting on a big show, playing military music for us. I carefully observed that what we encountered seemed to be no different from the airs of the League of Nations investigation team when they were observing in various parts of China. Our hearts were therefore deeply troubled.

When the train sped westward from Zheng, although it was dusk with dim clouds, and the night was gradually enveloping the surrounding earth, everyone was still excitedly watching the scenery outside the window. However, the same scenery was observed differently by each person. For example, when the train was traveling, everyone saw the distinctly independent yellow earth cliffs outside the train, of varying heights. Mr. Shen Yiqian, an artist, praised its unique scenery, saying it was worthy of sketching. Mr. Liu Zhonghe, a soil scientist, paid attention to the soil composition, believing it to be very fertile. Others took out ancient versions of Tang poems to verify historical sites in the field. It can be seen that the feelings, research, and future influences that arise from the same object vary from person to person.

From Zheng to Tongguan in the west, the abundance of historical sites is too numerous to recount. Twenty-two li north of the Tielu Station is the Zhou Ke Tomb, where Zhou Ke, the imperial censor of the Han Dynasty, and Ji Xin jointly defended Xingyang. When the city was broken, they were captured by Xiang Yu, and died unyielding. Thirty li south of Xingyang Station is the ancient city where Duke Zhuang of Zheng enfeoffed Duan. Sishui County, two li southeast of Sishui Station, is the Hulao Pass of Wei, which holds a very important place in ancient history. More than ten li south of Heishi Pass are the mausoleums of the emperors and empresses of the Song Dynasty. Eight li east of the station is said to be the Zhao Jin Tomb, nine li from the station is the Kou Laigong Tomb, and twelve li south of the station is the Bao Zheng Tomb. On the roadside south of Yanshi Station are the tombs of Boyi and Shuqi, and five li west of the station is the tomb of Yi Yin. More than ten li west of Yijingpu Station are the mausoleums of the emperors of the Han and Tang Dynasties. Luoyang was the ancient capital of the Zhou and Han dynasties. In the southwest of the city is the Zhougong Temple, and near the Baima Temple is the Di Liangong Tomb. Forty li southeast is the Fan Wenzhenggong Tomb, and the Shao Kangjie Ancestral Hall, the Er Cheng Xianxing Ancestral Hall, and the Guan Gong Tomb, etc. In addition, Mianchi was the place where ancient strategists used troops the most. Southwest of Lingbin City is the Guan Longfeng Tomb, and to its south is the Hangu Pass, where Laozi crossed westward. Tongguan spans the Elephant Mountain in the west and the Qilin Mountain in the southeast, with majestic terrain and many historical sites. The purpose of our westward journey this time is not to study antiques, but to conduct on-the-spot investigations of Shaanxi's industries using scientific methods, so we only describe the essentials.

Around 9:00 AM on the 12th, before we arrived at Tongguan, the Shaanxi Provincial Government had already sent Representative Xu and others to board the train to transport us to more than ten long-distance buses that had been prepared to transport us to Xi'an. Around 10:30 AM, we departed from Tongguan, with the South Route Director Hu Shuhua, Deputy Director Zhao Guobin, Doctor Ye Jingxun, Clerks Xiao Xinwu and Xu Hongling, North Route Director Hu Boyuyuan, Deputy Directors Ma Jin and Liu Chenghou, Doctor Qin Enfu, and Clerks Ou Zhaobang, Yu Zhonggang, and Liao Zhengmiao, each leading all the members, departing in buses. The trip was about six hours, said to be about two hundred and ten li long. The bus road was all dirt road. After driving for two hours, dust billowed, and we could not recognize each other's faces in the car. People sat in the car as if in a stormy sea, bumping and jumping violently. It was better later. After passing Weinan, we felt very uncomfortable because we were covered in dust. We ordered the drivers to stop by the road one after another and went to Huaqing Pool for a bath. There were three pools, two large and one small. When we washed our feet, we silently recited the line "The cold weather grants a bath in Huaqing, beginning a new reception of grace," and could not help but feel relaxed. Around 6:00 PM, we finally arrived in Xi'an. The South Group stayed at the Chang'an Apartment, and the North Group stayed at the Northwest Hotel. The scheduled itinerary is to depart from Xi'an for inspection on the 15th.

On the road west of Tongguan, we only saw yellow earth on both sides, with sparse organisms. Due to the lack of water, the products in the fields were greatly affected. Shaanxi is a fertile land, but it only lacks a little water, almost leading to thousands of miles of red land and people living in misery. If anyone wants to seek the rapid progress of Shaanxi's agriculture in the future, the first step must be to make efforts to think about irrigation. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 71

▲District Bureau Agrees to Dredge the City River

Previously, the First District Office received instructions from the county government, based on the approval of the county party headquarters meeting, that the city river was silted up and the water flow was polluted, which hindered simple life. Please instruct the Public Security and Construction Bureaus of the First District Office to discuss appropriate measures together. The district convened the Public Security and Construction Bureaus, including Shen Jingyu and Dao Yi, on this day (18th) to discuss solutions. It was decided to divide the measures into two types: active and passive. Passive measures: (A) The Public Security Bureau issues a notice prohibiting the dumping of dirty debris into the river, with penalties for violators, and adds patrol boats to inspect the river at any time. If it is found that someone is dumping dirt into the river, the police will arrest and punish them. (B) The district office sends letters to the township chiefs and police to persuade households not to dump dirty debris into the river. Active measures: First, the Construction Bureau sends personnel to measure the riverbed, estimate the earthwork, and prepare a budget, which is submitted to the county government for approval. Then, local people are hired to organize a committee to discuss the implementation. In addition, the Director of the Public Security Bureau proposed to investigate the city's riverbank, where dung tanks are densely lined up, which hinders drinking water. How should this be banned? It was decided that since the dung tanks are set up in low places, which easily get water, it is necessary to prevent drinking water. Each household should raise the original dung tank and the dung outlet stone hole by two feet, and cover them to emphasize hygiene. The Public Security Bureau will issue a notice on these measures, and the district office will instruct the township police to persuade households. In addition, the Director of the Public Security Bureau proposed that citizen Cai Guanghui requested a strict ban on coarse paper production, using rice straw as raw material to wash in the river. How should this be banned? It was decided that since coarse paper production uses rice straw as raw material and washes it in the river, it is indeed easy to make the river turbid and hinder hygiene. The Public Security Bureau should investigate according to the previous proposal and report it to the county government, which will instruct the Second District Chief to report the location in detail, so that they can be ordered to move.

▲Wuxian Jingbao is Repeatedly Accused

The Wuxian Jingbao, a tri-daily newspaper founded by Wuxian resident Wu Guoxiong, has recently been sued by Ms. Zhu Xiuwen and Yu Yu Ru, etc., who first filed a private prosecution with the local court, accusing the newspaper's director, Wu Guoxiong, and editor, Zhang Mengjuan, of defamation. After receiving the report, the county government is conducting a thorough investigation.

The Wuxian Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association had a major corruption case. The Anti-Japanese Association was taken over on the 18th and work began immediately.

Wuxi 74

▲Private Production of Inferior Silkworm Seeds Exposed

The only sideline of the rural villages in our county is mulberry planting and silkworm breeding. Therefore, silkworm seed production farms are everywhere in the city and countryside. However, some people who are blinded by profit see the advantages of seed production and start privately producing inferior seeds with fake brands for sale. This is not uncommon. Recently, Hu Jigao, the town chief of the Fifth Town of the First District, combined with Ni Yunqing, Zhu Ruopeng, etc., using the Yong Sheng Seed Production Farm's horse brand trademark, privately produced inferior seeds and sold them at the Shanghai Hotel on Tongyun Road, making a lot of profit. Recently, the Yong Sheng Farm found out and immediately reported to the Silkworm Industry Control Office, requesting that personnel be sent to thoroughly investigate. After receiving the report, Director Ni immediately sent staff members Ye Jingfeng and Shan Dinghaiping to rush to the scene and seized 660 fake seed sheets, and arrested Zhu Ruopeng and sent him to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Director Hua immediately sent police to arrest Ni Yunqing and Hu Jixian and bring them to the bureau, and sent a document to the county government. Chief Wang opened the court for interrogation and ordered Ni Yunqing to be detained, and Hu Jishang and Zhu Ruopeng to be released on bail pending trial.

▲A Young Girl's Breasts Grow Two Feet Long

Li Cuizhen, a seventeen-year-old girl from the northern countryside of the county, suddenly developed unusually large breasts during puberty. At first, she kept it a secret due to shyness, but unexpectedly, they gradually expanded, and her breasts drooped. Although there was no pain or itching, they were about two feet long, more than twenty times larger than the breasts of ordinary women, which was very burdensome and inconvenient. She came to the city yesterday to seek treatment from Wang Haitao, a Western doctor on Lianyuan Street in the city. After diagnosis by Dr. Wang, it was found that she had excessively long mammary glands, which were difficult to treat. If surgery was used to cut them off, the incision would be too large and there would be many dangers. Moreover, this disease is rare in the medical field, so he did not treat her at that time and she left. Afterwards, Mr. Wang specially imitated the European and American joint research model and informed Western doctors Li Keluo, Zhu Pinshan, and Zhu Daozhou in the county to discuss medical theory in order to adopt appropriate treatment methods. At the same time, Chinese medicine doctors Zhang Zimin, Gao Shiliang, Zhou Jingshou, and Deng Yinqing heard about this and also searched through ancient and modern medical books for discussion.

Changzhou 75

▲Provincial Commissioner Comes to Changzhou to Clear Rent

After the war in Shanghai, the Wu County Government was ordered to collect rent to provide relief. Recently, the Department of Finance believed that the Wu County rent matters had not been resolved, so it specially sent Commissioner Hou Shanzhong to Changzhou on the 17th to handle the clearance of rent matters and limited it to the end of this month. Commissioner Hou is currently in contact with County Magistrate Zhang to discuss everything.

▲County Magistrate Zhang Severely Punishes the Police for Facilitating Smuggling

County Magistrate Zhang of Wu ordered the Public Security Bureau to send personnel to the police team to go to Nan Zhai Town to investigate and seize the Shouwan machinery. Zeng Du, nicknamed Mei Lanfang's mother, was arrested, but the principal and important documents had escaped with money in advance. After investigation, it was found that Yu Jinrong, a police officer in charge of facilitating smuggling, had gone to the countryside to inform in advance. County Magistrate Zhang was furious when he heard the news, and summoned the government police and detective team on the 17th to give a speech and limited them to three hours to hand over Yu Jinrong. He was subsequently arrested and sent to the court for interrogation.

Changshu 76

▲Robbery of Earth Occurs at the South Gate

Shao Nangang, the current manager of the Southern Inn outside Xian Gate, prepared two packages of opium, weighing 24 taels, for his master Jin Jianxin to smoke the other day. Unexpectedly, Wang Ziqiang, the assistant of the shop, had some opinions with Shao. The other day, a huge amount of money was missing from the account, suspected to have been embezzled by Shao, so he negotiated with him. In fact, this money was taken by the shop owner Jin Jianxin. Shao resented being wronged and took the earth out. Wang suspected that he was going to report to the bureau, so he rushed up to stop him and tried to snatch the opium in his hand. During a scuffle, one package suddenly fell to the ground. It happened to be seen by the nearby police officer, who twisted Shao. Wang saw that the situation was not good, picked up one package and fled into the inn. Shao Nangang could not get rid of the package in his hand. In a moment of desperation, he saw a vendor selling sugar taro on the street, and threw the package of earth into the sugar taro pot. The police officer fished in the pot and found a package of opium (some say it was flower paste). He was about to take it back to the bureau to report when a hooligan named Xu Gengsheng suddenly came and slapped the small package of opium out of the police officer's hand and fled into the inn. At that time, the police officer only had a corner of the package paper in his hand, with a little paste stain. He rushed into the inn and arrested Xu Gengsheng and took him to the Second Police Station of the Public Security Bureau. As a result, he was released on bail. Soon, many hooligans surrounded the entrance of the Southern Inn, clamoring for a reward. The inn gave them seven or eight yuan to disperse. Unexpectedly, someone secretly reported to the Public Security Bureau, saying that the patrol officer of the Second Station was suspected of colluding. Director Yin immediately telegraphed to inquire about the patrol officer Fang Desheng in charge. Fang had no choice but to summon a group of witnesses and send them to the Bureau. On the 16th, they were transferred to the County Justice Department. After interrogation by Examiner Chai, Patrolman Shen Peng (the original detective) suddenly changed his testimony, with words that were mostly in favor of the defendant. The report of the station also stated that Wang and Shao were colleagues, and this was entirely caused by a joke and there was no opium. However, the County Justice Department believed that this case was important and immediately detained the robber Xu Gengsheng for investigation and further verification. The Public Security Bureau has repeatedly had major cases in the Second Station where Patrolman Fang failed to report (two people drowned in the previous dragon boat race, and Fang's handling before and after was improper). Now that this has happened again, there will be severe punishment to show punishment. Alas, the prevalence of opium and the unbridled hooligans in Changshu can be seen from this.

▲Education Funds are Not Available, Schools Temporarily Postpone Classes

The education funds of this county have been in arrears for more than six months during the tenure of Director Gao Tinggui in the last semester. Later, the Department of Education appointed Zhou Fengjing to Changshu to take over. The education sector immediately inquired about the education funds. According to his statement, the arrears before June (i.e., during Gao's tenure) are old debts and will be planned to be repaid in installments. After June, the new director will be responsible for clearing them monthly without any more arrears. Therefore, the people in the education sector were very happy. Unexpectedly, after Zhou came to Changshu, only one term of funds for June was issued, and there was no guarantee for the funds for July. The future is bleak. Moreover, the newly appointed principals are required to clear all new and old debts for those who have resigned. However, the bureau has no funds at all. For example, the county middle school, rural normal school, and the principals of various primary schools have all been appointed, so they have not been able to take over. According to the intentions of the general primary school principals, since the new Director Zhou has expressed that he will not be in arrears, the education funds for July should be issued immediately, otherwise the classes will be temporarily postponed this year to avoid being burdened. According to the news from the Education Bureau, the urgently needed funds are: the first batch is more than 5,800 yuan in arrears for the county middle school, the second batch is more than 3,700 yuan in arrears to repay the rural teachers, the third batch is about 10,000 yuan in arrears for changing various schools, and the fourth batch is more than 20,000 yuan in recurring expenses for July, totaling more than 40,000 yuan. Director Zhou has been very busy contacting people these days. It is said that he has a guarantee for the first batch, but he has no way to deal with the others. However, not only the Director of the Education Bureau should be responsible for these funds, but also the County Magistrate. Now only the county middle school has a way to deal with the arrears, while other schools have no way to deal with it. How can this be called fair?

In order to promote and develop the national industry, the Ministry of Industry plans to hold a national industrial survey, which is organized by the International Trade Bureau. ▲Jiangsu Province Reorganizes the County Defense Regiments

The Jiangsu Provincial Defense Committee has strictly limited the reorganization of the county defense regiments to be completed before August 30. Those that are in preparation include Jurong and 10 other counties. Those that have not held them include Taicang and 26 other counties. The three categories of those that have held them, those that are in preparation, and those that have not held them are listed as follows: Those that have held them include Zhenjiang, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Jintan, Liyang, Shanghai, Chongming, Qidong, Haimen, Changshu, Kunshan, Wuxi, Jingjiang, Nantong, Rugao, Taixing, Baoying, Peixian, Suining, Yizheng, Xiaoxian, Pixian, and 25 other counties. Those that have not held them include Taicang, Jiangning, Lishui, Yangzhou, Songjiang, Nanhui, Fengxian, Chuansha, Jiading, Baoshan, Wujin, Yixing, Jiangyin, Huaiyin, Siyang, Lianshui, Gaoning, Xinghua, Gaoyou, Fengxian, Xuyi, Suqian, Donghai, Guanyun, Muyang, and Ganyu and 26 other counties.

Rugao 78

▲An Old Man Commits Suicide Due to a Quarrel

Ge Da, a cook outside the South Gate of Rugao, only had his old father and wife at home. His daily life was still comfortable. His father was over seventy years old, and he liked to drink and get angry at every turn. Yesterday, due to a trivial matter, he had a quarrel with his daughter-in-law. In a fit of anger, he suddenly hanged himself. By the time his family noticed, it was too late to save him.

▲A Surrendered Bandit is Suddenly Killed in Revenge

Ding Fengshan, a surrendered bandit from the Lugang District, suddenly returned to Rugao from Shanghai the other day and was killed in revenge by bandits. His body was found in the Gaojingtian. His family has reported it to the county and requested an investigation.

Nantong 79

▲Two Well-Known Bandits in the Western Countryside are Shot

Ren Qu Er, two well-known bandits in the western countryside of Nantong, have committed numerous crimes. They were captured in Liuqiao and taken to the county government for interrogation. They confessed and were sentenced to death. On the 17th, County Magistrate Zhang received a telegram from the provincial government approving the execution of the two bandits on Chengyao Road.

▲Banditry is Rampant at the Junction of Tonghai

In the towns of Xinzifu An, etc., which are adjacent to the two counties of Nantong and Haimen, bandits have recently been using green gauze curtains to gather and cause trouble. Gunshots are heard everywhere at night, and the area has entered a state of terror. District Chief Ding Ziyan of Yiyu came to the city to ask the county government to transfer troops to suppress the bandits because the local defense regiment was weak.

▲A Traveler Commits Suicide by Taking Poison Due to World-Weariness

Xu Shiyan, a resident of Taixian who was staying at Room 29 of the Huizhong Inn in the south of the city, committed suicide by swallowing opium in his room on the 16th. A suicide note stated that he was suffering from environmental pressure and was tired of the world. After the inn reported it to the county court for inspection, they provided a coffin for burial.

Hangzhou 80

▲The Assassination Squad Warns Gao Yitai

Gao Yitai in Hangzhou is the largest silk and cloth shop in the city. Previously, it was fined more than 1,000 yuan and had its 20,000 yuan security deposit confiscated by the Anti-Japanese Association for privately selling Japanese goods. Manager Fang Kunliang absconded and was captured and made to stand in a wooden cage for a day. The other day, the shop suddenly received letters from the Youth Blood Soul Assassination Squad and the Iron Heart Assassination Squad, stating that members had reported that the shop was selling enemy goods. Please publish a statement in the newspaper immediately, otherwise, the final means will be used to deal with it. The shop has now publicly stated that it will never sell enemy goods and can ask for a thorough investigation to avoid misunderstandings.

Shen Bao Education News Special Issue No. 4 of the National Sports Conference

The Third Day of the National Sports Conference 81

Yesterday, the review of proposals by various groups in the morning and afternoon proceeded smoothly.

In the evening, Zhang Zhijiang and others hosted a banquet, and the third general assembly will be held this morning.

The Reasons and Hopes for Convening a National Sports Conference Amid National Crisis: Zhong Lingxiu

The clamor for the preparation of the National Sports Conference has been intermittent for several years, but no actual opening had been seen. Unexpectedly, amidst this national crisis, the formal convening of the conference suddenly took place, like a bolt from the blue, invigorating people's spirits. It is indeed a most gratifying event for the future of national sports. However, upon closer reflection, why is the sports conference not held in times of peace and tranquility, but suddenly held when the nation is in dire straits? This is quite thought-provoking. After repeated investigation, I have gained some insight into the reasons.

Throughout our country's history in Asia, for thousands of years, "refined and cultured" has been regarded as the highest elegance. Coupled with unhealthy habits and a lack of attention to hygiene, people have become sallow and weak, and their spirits are depressed. Foreigners mock us as "sick men of East Asia," which is not entirely unjustified. When the imperial examination system was abolished and schools were established, the educational purpose included "promoting martial spirit," and the curriculum included "gymnastics." However, this was merely seen as imitating Europe, America, and Japan, and as a decoration to the curriculum. Emphasizing sports in name only is like "looking from outside the palace walls," without any practical benefit. After the founding of the Republic of China, schools at all levels began to pay some attention. In the past decade, although there has been some progress, the government has never had active and concrete proposals, and social perceptions are often narrow and superficial. Therefore, our country's sports have had no systematic structure, system, or consistent spirit in the past. New trends focus on ball games and track and field, with competition becoming frenzied and increasingly resembling the commercialization of sports in Europe and America. Old traditions emphasize national martial arts, sticking to old ways and unwilling to start research from a scientific perspective to seek fundamental and rational improvements. Superficially, domestic sports today seem to be slightly more vibrant and have made some progress compared to the past. However, compared with the organized and targeted promotion of sports in Europe, America, and Japan, the difference is as vast as the heavens. Other countries consider the development of national sports to be the foundation of all kinds of education, while our country regards it as an appendage to education. Other countries consider the training of national sports to be the driving force for increasing production efficiency, while our country regards it as a negligible activity. Other countries' sports are planned, targeted, orderly, unified, and spiritually focused, while ours are chaotic, disorganized, and each goes its own way. Therefore, others can be healthy, strong, resilient, capable, and far-reaching, while we are physically weak and cannot withstand complexity. In contrast, in terms of international competition, the outcome is clear. Victory or defeat is not determined solely on the battlefield but is practically demonstrated and verified. As the saying goes, "Spirit is the mother of enterprise," and "A strong spirit resides in a strong body." To put it another way, to have a strong spirit, one must have a strong body, and with a strong spirit, one can achieve great undertakings. Now, our country, as a nation with weak physical strength, wants to establish itself in the world of the 20th century and compete with the great powers for victory. How can we not encounter failures and lag behind in everything? Now that the country is in trouble and foreign aggression is frequent, let us think, "A person must first insult himself before others insult him." The arrival of foreign aggression is not only due to political, economic, and scientific inferiority but also because the people's physical strength is weak, their spirits are depressed, their morale is low, they lack perseverance, and they lack unity. This is one of the main reasons for attracting foreign aggression. Since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have wondered how a nation of only 60 million Japanese people could dare to invade our dignified Chinese nation of 400 million people. Even if we are seven against one, and final victory, no matter what, belongs to us in our hearts, we still seem to be "indifferent" to the disaster. It must be understood that if people who are physically weak, untrained, and unprepared compete with people who are physically strong, trained, and prepared, no matter how many there are, what is the point? This is something that the people of the country must deeply awaken to. The government authorities, aware of this, believe that the weakness of the people's physical strength and the depression of their spirits are the root cause of attracting foreign aggression in the near future and the root cause of a weak race and a weak country in the long run. Therefore, when the country is in dire straits and the national treasury is strained, it does not hesitate to raise huge sums of money to hold a national sports conference, bringing together sports experts from all over the country to discuss the direction and implementation steps of national sports in the future, as a good way to save the national crisis. This will give national sports in the future a plan, a goal, an organization, an opportunity for common development, and a direction for overall training. The entire nation will strive to exercise, strengthen their bodies, and protect the country and defend the people under a unified goal, to seek revenge and wipe out the humiliation, to resist foreign aggression, and to resolve the national crisis and stabilize the country. This is the fundamental purpose of convening the National Sports Conference amidst national crisis, which I believe is understood by all the participants. I respectfully hope that all the participants will express their great opinions and carefully discuss how to develop national sports, promote national spirit, resolve the national crisis, and save the national crisis as their duty. Weigh the world situation, consider the national conditions, formulate good plans, and ensure that the conference is held, discussions are made, decisions are made, decisions are implemented, and implementation is widespread. In a few years, the achievements of all the participants will spread throughout the country and resonate at home and abroad. This is what we sincerely pray for and what the people of the whole country earnestly hope for.

Review by Various Groups 82

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. Starting at 8:00 AM on the 18th, various groups held sub-group review meetings at the Lizhi Society in the morning and afternoon. After each group completed its review, it prepared a report to be submitted to the general assembly. After the resolution, it was submitted to the National Physical Education Implementation Plan Organizing Committee for consideration and inclusion in the plan, in order to complete the "National Physical Education Implementation Plan." The review situation of each group is recorded as follows:

In addition, the Target Group, because it needed to withdraw the Six-Character Doctrine proposal, decided to hold another review meeting on the afternoon of the 19th.

(2) The Third Meeting of the Administrative Organization Group

▲ Request to restore the Third Section of the Social Education Department

▲ Education Departments and Bureaus should establish Sports Committees

▲ Add a Sports Section to the Social Education Section

▲ The Central Sports Field should be directly under the Ministry of Education

▲ Change the name of the sports field to include the province, city, and county name

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. The administrative group held a review meeting in the morning and afternoon of the 18th, chaired by Yuan Dunli. Resolutions: (1) Merge the thirteen proposals submitted by Wu Zhongjun and others into a proposal that sports supervisors should be set up in educational administrative organs at all levels; (2) Merge the three proposals from the alumni association of the Physical Education Department of Central University and others into the proposal that the Ministry of Education, departments, and bureaus should each establish sports committees, and add sports sections to the social education departments to be responsible for the design of school and social sports in their respective jurisdictions, and administrative matters. The Ministry of Education shall establish a National Sports Committee and restore the original Third Section of the Social Education Department. The Department of Education and the Special City Education Bureau shall establish Provincial and Municipal Sports Committees, and add sports sections to the Social Education Section. Ordinary city and county education bureaus shall establish city and county sports committees, and add sports sections to the social education section. In addition, the Central Sports Field should be directly under the Ministry of Education to preserve the entire education system. The existing "Public" characters in the names of the sports fields in various provinces, cities, and counties should be uniformly removed and named "Provincial, City, and County Sports Field" to unify the names. (3) The proposal of Liu Tianzhen to streamline the national sports administrative system to facilitate progress was resolved to submit a summary to the general assembly for reference. (4) The proposal of the Jingwu Sports Association that public sports fields in various provinces, cities, and counties should set up national martial arts instructors to be responsible for the work was resolved to be changed to "Sports fields in various provinces, cities, and counties should set up national martial arts departments to promote it." (5) The proposal of Jia Zizheng to promote the authority of the executive organs of school sports administration was resolved to be retained. (6) The proposal of Zhang Pei to request the Central Government to urge remote provinces to quickly establish national martial arts halls to preserve the national essence and promote the national spirit was resolved to be submitted to the Implementation and Promotion Group for review and submitted to the Evaluation Group for reference. (7) The proposal of Zhou Fohai to promote the systematic organization of sports in various provinces, cities, and counties to facilitate promotion was resolved to be left for discussion in the various sports organizations and club sections.

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. The Second Group continued to meet in the afternoon of the 18th, chaired by Yuan Dunli. It was resolved that the chairman should report to the general assembly. (1) Continue to discuss the funding proposal, and it was resolved to revise it as follows: The sports funds of schools at all levels, in addition to the sports fees paid by students, should be a fixed budget, and the amount should be at least 5% of the total school funds, and submit it to the general assembly together with opinions. (2) It is proposed to levy a tax on luxury goods and hobbies to promote the foundation of sports and national martial arts. It was resolved to submit it to the general assembly for reference. (3) Regarding the assembly organization section, it was resolved that the National Games should be held every two years, and the Ministry of Education's National Sports Committee should designate provinces to hold it in rotation. (4) The proposal to hold sports meetings once a year in various provinces, cities, and counties was resolved to be retained. (5) The 1st, 6th, and 20th proposals were resolved to be merged into the following: Athletes participating in sports meets at all levels and of all kinds must first undergo a review of their academic performance, character, age, physical condition, and amateur qualifications. The standards and methods shall be researched and stipulated by the Sports Committee of the Ministry of Education. (6) The 16th proposal was resolved to be submitted to the Competition and Sports Regulations Committee of the Ministry of Education for research and revision together with other rules.

(5) General Report of the Evaluation Group

▲ Before the implementation standards for sports are promulgated

▲ Each province should first stipulate temporary standards

▲ The Examination Yuan lists sports as a required subject

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. Fifth Group Review General Report: (A) Proposals related to the evaluation group include: 1. The evaluation of sports achievements in our country today should focus on testing. It was resolved that this case can be used as a principle for evaluation. (1) Strictly implement sports standards. (2) Students in schools at all levels who fail sports may not graduate. (3) Sports in schools at all levels should be ordered by the Ministry of Education to the provincial education departments to order their affiliated schools that students who fail the subject should not be promoted or graduate. It was resolved that the above three cases should be discussed together, and the case should be changed to "Strictly implement sports standards." The reasons and methods should also use the reasons and methods of the first case, and add "However, before the Ministry of Education promulgates the standards, each province and city may formulate temporary standards according to local conditions to facilitate progress." (4) Please ask the Examination Yuan to stipulate that all levels and types of examinations must select the sports technology subject as a required subject to promote it and strengthen the people. It was resolved to change the "select" word in this case to "use" and remove the three words "technical subject." (5) 1. School sports should focus on the general improvement of the health of all students. 2. Please pay attention to university sports as the promotion of school sports. It was resolved that the above two cases should be discussed together, and the methods should be merged into this group's "My son's evaluation of sports achievements in the future should focus on testing." According to the above review results, the principles and methods for determining sports evaluation are as follows: (1) Principles: 1. Average development in terms of individuals, 2. Universal testing in terms of groups, 3. Universal testing in terms of society. (2) Methods: 1. Strictly implement sports standards, but before the Ministry of Education promulgates the standards, each province has to formulate temporary standards according to local conditions to facilitate progress, 2. Use the testing method to evaluate sports achievements, 3. Please ask the Examination Yuan to stipulate that all types of examinations must include sports as a required subject. (B) Rewarding and guiding public sports case, transferred to the administrative organization group. (C) Rewarding national sports case, transferred to the implementation and promotion group.

Organize the East China University Association 90

18th Telegram from Nanjing. Zhang Xinfu and seventeen other sports directors from universities in East China held a discussion meeting at Lizhi Society on the 18th and decided to organize the East China University Sports Association, not only to promote university sports technology but also to focus on the cultivation of sports ethics and guide the popularization of sports in primary and secondary schools in East China, and promote public sports. Chu Minyi Discusses the National Games 91

—First divide each region and hold regional games every year—

—The National Games will be held once every three years—

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. Chu Minyi said that the National Games are difficult to convene due to the size of China. It is best to first divide East China, North China, and South China into three regions, and each region will hold them in rotation once. After each region has been held, the National Games will be convened in the capital once every three years, so that the sports achievements of each region can be compared. The convener of the Regional Games should be the Sports Committee of the provinces and cities in the region, and the convener of the National Games should be the Sports Committee of the Ministry of Education. The Administrative Group of the 18th resolved that the National Games should be held once every two years and should be convened in rotation in the provinces designated by the Sports Committee of the Ministry of Education.

He Yingqin Plans to Run a Private Sports School 92

—The address is near the Central Sports Field—

—The funding is 20,000 and Zhang Xinfu is entrusted with the plan—

Nanjing, 18th Telegram. He Yingqin plans to establish a private sports school near the Central Sports Field to train sports teachers for primary and secondary schools. The start-up cost is 20,000 yuan. Zhang Xinfu was entrusted with drafting the plan, and Zhang started planning after the plenary meeting.

Female Expert Zhang Huilan Discusses Women's Sports 93

—Men's sports cannot be applied to women—

—Women's sports should be guided by women—

—Seek sports that are suitable for women—

Nanjing, 18th Telegram, Zhang Huilan, a female expert, was elected as the female representative in the program organizing committee. The reporter visited her before the meeting and selected her views on women's sports. The main points of the conversation are as follows: I participated in the meeting this time to improve the women's sports program. Some members misunderstood that I meant that sports should be divided into men and women. This is not my original intention. I think that women's sports should be stipulated within the scope of what women's body and mind can do, and cannot be based on men's perspectives. As for the meaning of sports, there are two: (1) for health, (2) for education. Health seeks universality, not competition. Using men's standards to force women to do strenuous sports competitions will hinder the development of women's physiology. In terms of education, teachers and students are not only teacher-student relationships but also have the obligation of life guidance. If men are responsible for women's sports teachers, it will not only be useless but also harmful. In general, my opinions are two: (1) Stipulate the scope of sports according to women's physiology. (2) Female sports instructors are most suitable for women.
