Draft of National Physical Education Implementation Plan (4) 95

(1) Biological Sciences, including subjects such as anatomy, physiology, hygiene, first aid, massage, health checkups, exercise physiology, account for ...... 19%

(2) Educational Sciences, including subjects such as introduction to education, educational psychology, teaching methods, educational administration, educational philosophy, health education, police education, account for ...... 15%

(3) Physical Education Theory, including subjects such as principles of physical education, principles of games, physical education administration, physical education teaching methods, elementary school teaching materials, kinesiology, physical education history, mass physical education, account for ...... 20%

(4) Skills ...... account for 21%

(5) Cultural subjects and electives ...... account for 25%

Those who have received the above four years of university training are mostly employed in secondary or higher schools. As for the training of elementary school physical education teachers, a physical education group or elective course should be established within the normal school. In addition to the physical education that normal school students should learn, those who aspire to be physical education teachers must take the following courses as electives, which must include at least the following:

(1) Physical Education (including principles, management methods, and teaching methods, etc.)

(2) Preparation and practice of elementary school physical education teaching materials

(3) Physical education teaching practice

B. Standards for Physical Education Teacher Training Institutions

(1) Qualifications of Teachers

A. Assistant Teacher

Graduation from a domestic or foreign university with a bachelor's degree and with considerable academic achievements.

B. Lecturer

Graduation from a domestic or foreign university with a master's degree and with considerable academic achievements.

C. Associate Professor

Having served as a teacher for more than one year and having special achievements, or having studied at a foreign university for several years and obtained a doctoral degree with considerable academic achievements.

Lecturer having served as a teacher for more than one year and having special achievements.

D. Professor

Associate Professor having served as a teacher for more than two years and having special achievements.

(2) Qualifications of Students: High school graduates who have passed the general university entrance examination.

(3) Equipment

A. Two playgrounds or gymnasiums, including at least one basketball court, and equipped with various indoor exercise equipment.

B. Sports field, 400-meter running track and track and field equipment (including football and baseball).

C. Three basketball courts.

D. Four netball courts.

E. Chinese martial arts room and various equipment.

F. Anatomy and physiology laboratory and equipment.

G. Specialized books and magazines.

As for the physical education teachers hired by normal schools that train elementary school physical education teachers, they must be graduates of a university physical education department or graduates of a university physical education major with more than three years of study and considerable experience.

C. Continuing Education Methods for Current Physical Education Teachers

(1) Summer School: The Ministry of Education designates domestic universities to take turns running summer schools, and the Ministry of Education subsidizes the expenses.

(2) Physical Education Research Institute: The Ministry of Education designates physical education departments with achievements to prepare for additional establishment.

D. Sending Physical Education Teachers with Excellent Achievements to Study Abroad

(1) The Education Departments of each province shall establish physical education scholarships. Applicants must have the following qualifications to be eligible for application:

A. Graduates of a university physical education department who have served for more than two years.

B. University graduates who have served for more than five years and have made significant achievements in physical education.

(2) The central government shall send physical education experts to foreign countries for investigation and research every three years.

(3) Standards for Implementation of Physical Education 96

(A) School Physical Education

I. Physical Education Curriculum

(1) Universities: Although the university curriculum standards have not yet been promulgated by the Ministry of Education, physical education should be a required subject for all grades, and students who fail shall not be allowed to graduate.

(2) Primary and Secondary Schools and Normal Schools: Schools at all levels shall follow the provisional curriculum standards of the Ministry of Education, and students who fail the graduation examination shall not be allowed to graduate.

II. Teacher Qualifications

(1) Universities: Graduates of university physical education departments.

(2) Secondary Schools and Normal Schools: Graduates of university physical education departments or physical education majors with more than three years of study.

(3) Elementary Schools: Graduates of normal schools or physical education vocational schools.

(B) Mass Physical Education: Although mass physical education has been promoted for many years, it has not yet become popular. There are still few adults who have an interest in physical education and considerable skills, especially in remote towns and cities. Therefore, to promote mass physical education, one aspect should start with children, and small-scale children's playgrounds should be set up in many towns and cities. On the other hand, physical education facilities that are of interest to the public, such as stone locks and swords, should be attached to these playgrounds.

(4) Promoting and Rewarding Various Types of Physical Education Gatherings and Organizations 97

Private physical education organizations in our country's society, such as the National Physical Education Advancement Association, the North China Physical Education Federation, and the Advancement Associations and Federations in major cities, all have a long history and considerable achievements. As for other sporadic competitions and sports meets, they are even more popular for a time. Although there are few physical education conferences for observing technology and research associations for studying physical education academics, they are gradually gaining momentum. On the one hand, the government should not abandon its right to supervise these organizations to improve their standards. On the other hand, it must give them considerable encouragement to strive for their universality among the people. Therefore, the government must strictly define the standards and management methods for the protection of physical education gatherings and organizations, and at the same time, it should provide considerable assistance to those who have achieved success, and find ways to enlighten those areas without such organizations. The following draft is hereby stipulated:

I. The organization of various sports federations, whether temporary or permanent, must meet the following standards and be filed with the competent educational authority:

(1) The purpose is pure and purely amateur.

(2) The competition must have appropriate age and gender classifications.

(3) The responsible organizers must have served in the physical education field for more than two years and have considerable achievements.

(4) The participating units are definitely representatives of educational or vocational institutions and are not engaged in sports as a profession and do not hinder the amateur spirit.

(5) There is a definite budget and the income from tickets is not used to cover maintenance costs.

II. If the groups filed in the above paragraph continue to operate for three years and the competent educational authority considers that they have made considerable achievements, they may be given spiritual and material assistance. If, after filing, there is a violation of the above regulations, measures may be taken to ban them. The ban method shall be handled separately according to the severity of the circumstances.

III. Various groups for observing technology must have the following qualifications to be filed with the competent educational authority:

(1) All members have legitimate occupations and are not engaged in sports as a profession.

(2) There are physical education experts to provide guidance.

(3) Participation in various competitions or sports does not use ticket revenue to cover maintenance costs or be apportioned to members.

(4) Members only have the obligation to pay fees and do not enjoy material rights.

IV. If the above groups have special achievements after filing, they may be given considerable rewards. If there is a violation of the standards set in the above paragraph, the qualification of the group and all its members will be cancelled.

V. Groups in items (1) and (3) that have not been filed with the competent educational authority shall not participate in various gatherings and competitions organized by the educational authority and filed groups.

VI. Organizations whose purpose is to study physical education academics and have definite achievements may register with the educational authority in accordance with the methods for academic groups and may be given considerable subsidies.

VII. In areas where there are no physical education organizations, the competent educational authority shall convene people in the physical education field to promote the organization.

VIII. Various groups that have been filed may report to the competent educational authority in advance for review and consideration of subsidies when participating in international gatherings or sports meets.

IX. Various physical education groups shall not participate in political activities in the name of the group.

Female members, Gu Guxi, left, and Huang Liming, right (photographed by Guanghua, Nanjing)

(5) Methods for Assessing Physical Education: The assessment of physical education has an opposite position to sports meets. Sports meets assess individual achievements and are only enough to promote the progress of individual achievements. Using this as a standard for judging the entire physical education of schools and the public is actually a mistake. Even using this as a tool for promotion, hoping to popularize physical education in schools and among the public is like climbing a tree to catch a fish. On the contrary, the physical education assessment is to examine the physical education achievements of all the citizens in a school or city, which can urge the progress of the physical education of the majority of the public. Using this as a means to evaluate the physical education of schools or cities is very reliable.

A. The assessment committee can be divided into three types: national, provincial, and county, according to the administrative organization.

I. The National Physical Education Assessment Committee shall be organized by the Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education by hiring domestic physical education experts.

(1) Investigate the physical education of national universities and registered private universities in the country, determine their order of precedence, and announce it.

(2) Determine the physical education achievements of each province and announce them.

II. The Provincial Physical Education Assessment Committee shall be organized by the Provincial Physical Education Supervisor by hiring physical education experts (if necessary, it can be divided into several districts, and assessment committees can be organized separately).

(1) Investigate the physical education achievements of provincial middle schools, normal schools, and vocational schools in the province and report to the Education Department.

(2) Investigate the physical education achievements of graduates of provincial senior high schools, junior high schools, normal schools, and vocational schools.

(3) Investigate the mass physical education of provincial cities, report the number and percentage of those who pass the examination and participate to the Education Department.

III. The County Physical Education Assessment Committee shall be organized by the Education Bureau of each county or physical education teachers from neighboring counties.

(1) Investigate the physical education achievements of county-run primary and secondary schools in the county, determine the order of precedence, and announce it, and report the achievements of secondary schools to the Education Department.

(2) Investigate the physical education achievements of graduating students from senior high schools, junior high schools, normal schools, and vocational schools in the county.

(4) Investigate the achievements of mass physical education in the county and report to the Education Department.

B. Assessment items shall be designated for research by research institutions.

C. The standards for assessment shall be obtained through research by research institutions. D. Types of assessment:

I. Graduation Examinations for Students at All Levels

(1) Elementary School: According to the elementary school physical education graduation standards, those who fail shall not be allowed to graduate.

(2) Middle School, Normal School, and Vocational School: According to the middle school physical education graduation standards, those who fail shall not be allowed to graduate.

(3) University: According to the university physical education graduation standards, those who fail shall not be allowed to graduate.

II. School Physical Education Achievement Examination

(1) Elementary School: Conducted by the County Physical Education Assessment Committee, the Education Bureau determines the order and announces it.

(2) Middle School, Normal School, and Vocational School: Conducted by the Provincial or County Physical Education Committee, reported to the Education Department, determined and announced by the Education Department.

(3) University: The examination is conducted by the Physical Education Assessment Committee of the province where the university is located, reported to the Ministry of Education, and determined and announced by the Ministry of Education.

Five-Year Implementation Plan 98

The physical education facilities and promotion methods listed in this plan cannot be completed overnight under the current situation in our country. Therefore, it is necessary to divide the implementation into phases based on economic resources, talents, and local conditions. A phased implementation plan is hereby drafted for reference by the competent authorities.

The Following Should Be Implemented in the First Year: 99

(1) Completion of the central and local administrative organizations.

(2) The central government and each province shall determine the physical education budget.

(3) The current expenses of schools at all levels in cities must be implemented according to the established standards.

(4) Mass physical education venues shall be established in major cities.

(5) Various research projects shall begin, and research institutions shall submit research plans.

(6) The curriculum and standards for talent training shall be promulgated.

(7) Summer schools shall be prepared and operated.

(8) Measures for filing and rewarding physical education groups shall be promulgated and implemented in practice.

(9) Each province shall set up a physical education scholarship quota as appropriate.

(10) Schools at all levels shall appropriately increase physical education equipment.

(11) It is reiterated that physical education shall be a required subject for schools at all levels, and those who fail shall not be allowed to graduate.

(12) Each province may conduct trial assessment methods.

The Following Should Be Completed Within the Third Year: 100

(1) Various research projects should have considerable results reports and be implemented.

(2) Mass physical education venues shall be established in each county.

(3) Physical education equipment in schools at all levels shall reach two-thirds of what is stipulated in this plan.

(4) The central government shall send several physical education experts to various countries for research and investigation once, for a period of one year.

(5) Conduct achievement assessments in major cities and towns.

The Following Should Be Completed Within the Fifth Year: 101

(1) Physical education venues in various villages.

(2) Physical education equipment in schools at all levels shall reach the standards of this plan.

(3) Conduct achievement assessments nationwide.

(4) Research projects should have considerable results.

The above plan should be supervised and implemented by the Central Physical Education Committee. After the five-year period expires, the Second National Physical Education Conference should be convened to stipulate the implementation methods for the future. The current plan cannot be valid for more than five years. (End)

Division of China Public School After Announcing Temporary Suspension 102

China Public School has internal complexities and frequent turmoil. The board of directors, considering the difficulty of reorganization and the lack of anyone willing to serve as principal, announced that it would temporarily suspend operations for the next semester. The disposal methods for students are divided into two categories: borrowing and transferring. Students in the third and fourth years of the university department will be issued a borrowing certificate by the school to borrow and study at other schools. In the future, after completing the credits, they will still graduate from the school. Students in the first and second grades of the university department and students in the high school department will be issued transfer certificates and transcripts, allowing students to freely transfer to other schools. As for the freshmen who did not take the entrance examination in the previous semester, they are considered borrowing students and are issued transcripts, allowing them to return to their original schools to study.

Local News

Unreasonable Interference by Japanese Consulate on People's Patriotic Movement Day 107

▲ A Written Protest Was Lodged the Day Before Yesterday Afternoon

▲ Mayor Wu Promised to Consider and Reply

Since the activities of the Blood Soul Eliminate Traitors Group and others in this city, the treacherous merchants who operate Japanese goods have disappeared and have asked the Japanese side for returns, resulting in a great blow to Japanese trade with China. According to the results of the investigation by the Japanese Businessmen's Association, the indirect and direct losses suffered in the recent month due to the activities of the Blood Soul Eliminate Traitors Group and others in Shanghai alone have reached about one million yuan. Therefore, representatives have been sent to the Consul-General in Shanghai, Murai, to petition, requesting that a protest be lodged with our municipal government. At the same time, a telegram was sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Tokyo, requesting that direct negotiations be made with our Ministry of Foreign Affairs. On the 13th of this month, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed the Consul-General in Shanghai, Murai, ordering him to immediately comply with the wishes of the overseas Chinese and lodge a practical protest with our municipal government to stop it. After receiving the order, Consul Murai immediately drafted a protest letter and went to the Shanghai Municipal Government in Fenglin Bridge at 4:30 pm the day before yesterday (17th) with Vice-Consul Shirai to lodge the protest with Mayor Wu in person. Mayor Wu personally extended the meeting. According to Murai, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce recently telegraphed various industry groups across the country to refuse to purchase Japanese goods, which has had a profound impact on Japan's entire trade with China. In addition, the activities of the Blood Soul Eliminate Traitors Group and others have made the people of China and Japan feel animosity. Therefore, he specially lodged a protest with your Mayor, requesting that appropriate measures be taken to stop it in order to increase friendly relations between the two countries, etc. However, Mayor Wu did not give a definite indication at that time, but promised to consider it and reply later. The two sides talked until 5:45 before dispersing.

▲ Mayor Wu Talks to Reporter of the Newsound Agency: According to Mayor Wu, Consul-General Murai of Japan came to the government yesterday to protest the anti-Japanese goods movement in this city. I replied at the time that if there are any irregular or illegal actions, the municipal government will take measures to stop them in accordance with the law. If it is within the reasonable scope of the people's movement, the municipal government will not be able to stop them. However, the formal reply is still under consideration. As for the people's patriotism, it must be automatic and motivated by conscience, and it must be an orderly action. Do not be motivated by emotions and only engage in empty talk, which will cause other problems and make it difficult for the government authorities, etc.

▲ Deputy Consul of Japan Talks to Reporter of the Times News Agency: After learning that the Japanese side had lodged a written protest with the municipal government regarding the patriotic movement of our people, he drove to the Japanese Consulate at 3 pm yesterday to inquire about everything. Deputy Consul Shirai came out to meet him. The reporter then had the following conversation with him: Reporter (Q): Yesterday (that is, the day before yesterday), your Consul went to the municipal government to protest to Mayor Wu, requesting that the activities of the Blood Soul Eliminate Traitors Group and others be stopped. Can you tell us the content of the protest letter? Shirai (A): The scope of the written protest lodged with your Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday was to request appropriate measures to stop the activities of the Blood Soul Eliminate Traitors Group. At the same time, a request was also attached to dissuade your government from the telegram issued by your Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to various industries to refuse to purchase Japanese goods, because this telegram from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is tantamount to a fatal blow to our country's trade with your country. (Q) Did your Mayor Wu give a definite reply at that time? (A) There was no definite reply, but he promised to wait for consideration in a short period of time and then give a written reply. (Q) A Japanese newspaper in Shanghai recently published a slanderous message stating that more than 80 policemen from our side stationed at the Baziqiao in Zhabei had absconded. Our Shanghai Municipal Government has already lodged a protest with your consulate, requesting that a practical correction be made and that such incidents not occur again in the future. Has your consulate notified the newspaper to do so? (A) This matter can be said to have been resolved, because after receiving your protest, our consulate immediately notified the newspaper to follow the instructions of your municipal government. (Q) Your country's naval landing force stationed in Shanghai has repeatedly armed and crossed the border to demonstrate. Our Shanghai Municipal Government has already lodged a protest with your consulate, but we have not yet received a definite reply from your consulate. How will this matter be handled? Can you tell us? (A) This case is still under detailed investigation by our consulate. However, your protest to our consulate, stating that our landing force crossed the border to demonstrate many times, does not seem accurate. It is true that our landing force was ordered to be transferred to the area of the road built across the border on North Sichuan Road, but if it is necessary to pass through your territory, your Public Security Bureau will be formally notified in advance to avoid misunderstandings. Therefore, the protest lodged by your Shanghai Municipal Government to our consulate, even if it is a fact, cannot be called a cross-border demonstration, because our landing force headquarters had previously sent a notification to your Public Security Bureau. As for the news published in your newspaper today that our landing force is demonstrating on Zhongshan Road again, this matter is completely untrue, because a team of our landing force stationed in Shanghai was recently ordered by Commander Sugisaka to go to the Toyota Spinning Mill on Zhongshan Road to replace the soldiers stationed in the factory, which led your people to mistakenly believe that it was a cross-border demonstration. According to the armistice agreement signed between China and Japan on May 23, it was also stated that "Japanese soldiers can pass through the Chinese territory if they want to go to the Toyota Spinning Mill on Zhongshan Road." Therefore, the various sections published in your newspaper today are obviously rumors.

National Government Recognizes Chilean Government 108

▲ Sino-Chilean Trade Treaty Negotiations to Begin Next Month

It is recently heard that China and Chile will soon begin negotiations on a new friendly trade treaty. However, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency, believing that recognition of the new Chilean government is a prerequisite before China and Chile formally begin these negotiations, visited Mr. Fei Bailai, the Chargé d'Affaires of Chile in China, at the Chilean Legation yesterday. The details of the Chargé d'Affaires' statements are recorded below:

▲ Recognition of the Chilean Government: According to Mr. Fei Bailai, Chargé d'Affaires and Consul-General of Chile in China, Chile has established a sound new government after a revolution. On the 8th of last month, he received instructions from the new government and immediately notified the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting recognition. On the 16th of the same month, he received a reply from Mr. Luo Wengan, Minister of Foreign Affairs of China, formally recognizing the new Chilean government and expressing that China and Chile would continue their previous friendly spirit and work to enhance the friendship between the two countries. He immediately telegraphed the report to his home government, and the entire Chilean nation expressed their deep gratitude for this.

▲ Negotiation of a Commercial Treaty Between the Two Countries: Mr. Fei Bailai said that the proposal for China and Chile to negotiate a commercial and friendly treaty originated in 1929. In Santiago, Chile, the Chinese Chargé d'Affaires in Chile, Mr. Zhang, contacted the Chilean government. Later, before formal negotiations could begin, Mr. Zhang was transferred to Switzerland and left Chile. Subsequently, I was ordered to come to China in the summer of last year, and the negotiation was moved to China. Last time, when Vice Minister Guo Taiqi was in Shanghai, I contacted him several times. Mr. Guo then ordered Mr. Zhang Sixu, Director of the Intelligence Department, to conduct research on behalf of him. Recently, after receiving instructions from the new Chilean government, I immediately notified the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to request a scheduled formal negotiation. Later, it was stalled due to the resignation of Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan. Now that this matter is expected to be resolved, I believe the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will select an appropriate date and begin negotiations. According to observations, it is expected that it may begin around September.

▲ Friendly Overseas Chinese in Both Countries: The Chargé d'Affaires recalled what he told a reporter from the New Voice News Agency when he first arrived in China, saying that there are approximately 100 to 200 Chinese residing in Chile, mostly living in the southern provinces of China. Most of the Chinese who travel to Chile are scattered in the northern provinces of Chile, with a population of approximately 2,000. The overseas Chinese in both countries are friendly with the local people. The Chinese are quite settled, and the Chilean government treats them no differently than its own citizens.

▲ Chilean Legation to Move: The Shanghai office of the Chilean Legation and Consulate is currently located at No. 54, Sevastopulo Apartments, 131 Avenue des Soeurs. Recently, the Chargé d'Affaires decided to move to a new location at No. 400 Route Haig next Wednesday because the current location is insufficient.

Large Batch of Chinese Silk Shipped to the United States Yesterday 109

▲ More Than 700 Pieces Shipped to New York

▲ Artificial Silk Stagnant Due to Increased Taxes

Since the boom in artificial silk sales, Chinese silk exports have suffered a major blow. The European and American silk markets have been further squeezed by Japanese silk. The export volume of Huzhou silk from China has fallen sharply. Due to the sharp drop in silk prices, various silk factories have stopped work one after another. Due to cost considerations, most of the silk stored last year has not been sold, and silk merchants have suffered heavy losses. In order to rescue the silk industry and encourage exports, the central government has increased the tax rate on artificial silk on the one hand, and exempted the consolidated tax and export tax on Chinese silk on the other hand. Furthermore, it has subsidized 100 taels of silver per piece of exported silk to show its utmost effort to save the situation. Since the implementation of these measures, the American silk market has gradually become active, and large quantities of Chinese silk, which had been stagnant for more than a year, have begun to be exported, which is good news for the future of the silk industry.

▲ Government Relief: The Ministry of Finance, responding to the requests of various silk merchants, has noted that various factories in Shanghai have a large amount of stored silk, all of which are old goods from last year. The cost of each piece of factory silk must be between 800 and 900 taels, or even 1,000 taels. At the current market price, each piece must lose 400 or 500 taels. In order to rescue the silk industry, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Jianghai Customs to exempt the consolidated tax and export tax on all exported Chinese silk, starting from this month. The Silk Industry Relief Office established by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is even more rewarding for Chinese silk exports, with a subsidy of 100 taels of silver per piece of Chinese silk shipped to European and American countries, in addition to tax exemption. Since the implementation of these two measures, silk merchants have benefited greatly. Selling one piece of Huzhou silk can reduce losses by 150 or 160 taels.

▲ 700 Pieces of Chinese Silk Shipped to the United States: Chinese silk shipments to the United States have been stagnant for nearly a year. Recently, they have gradually become active. Various silk factories in Shanghai have purchased more than 1,000 pieces of yellow and white factory silk from American merchants in recent days. Today, they began loading the President McKinley of the Great American Lines, bound for New York, USA, with approximately 700 pieces. The exported silk was declared yesterday and will be loaded onto the ship in the Huangpu River this morning. This is the first batch of Chinese silk exports that have been stalled for a year and has obtained the benefits of tax exemption and government subsidies.

▲ Artificial Silk Accumulation: A large amount of artificial silk has been imported in recent years, which has greatly affected domestic silk. Since the customs increased taxes, the import tax on artificial silk must be 50% of the value. On the 4th of this month, the Ministry of Finance announced new tariff regulations, and the import tax on artificial silk increased by another 30%, totaling 80% of the value. Plus an additional surcharge of 14%, the total import tax on artificial silk is 94%. Due to the sharp increase in import taxes, various Italian trading companies in Shanghai that deal in artificial silk have sent telegrams to their home countries to stop ordering. The agents of the foreign trading companies are also unwilling to pay this huge tax and have transferred large quantities of artificial silk to the customs warehouse. In recent days, the fourth and eighth customs warehouses of the Shanghai Customs have been filled with foreign artificial silk. Since August 4th, various firms in this city that deal in artificial silk have changed their methods. For those who purchase this product, they report and withdraw a certain number of pieces to the customs temporarily. In this way, they can avoid prepaying huge taxes. However, due to the accumulation in the Jianghai Customs, large quantities of this foreign artificial silk will no longer be shipped in.

Huang Tingyu Describes Improved Flying Arrow Plan 110

▲ Iron-Blooded National Salvation Army Concentrated in Kailu

▲ Ammunition Running Out, Hoping for Support from All Sectors

Huang Tingyu, the inventor of the Flying Arrow, previously came to Shanghai with Yin Kaisan, the commander-in-chief of the Northeast Iron-Blooded National Salvation Army, to test the Flying Arrow. The results were good. Mr. Huang and Mr. Yin are currently in contact with all sectors to seek assistance for the National Salvation Army's military affairs. They will not be able to return north for about a week. According to Mr. Yin, the Northeast Iron-Blooded National Salvation Army has three armies. The first army is led by General Yin Chuan and has approximately 7,000 cavalrymen. It is currently concentrated in the provinces of Rehe and Chahar, desperately starting out. A report from the army states that the Li Division of the army, with more than 2,000 soldiers, has been concentrated in Kailu. It is currently short of ammunition and will launch an attack immediately after receiving ammunition. The second army is led by Yin Yuanmin and has approximately 7,000 infantry and cavalrymen. It is currently scattered in the Haicheng, Yingkou, and Dashiqiao areas and is fighting fiercely with the enemy. The army is also running out of ammunition and urgently needs supplies. The third army is led by Zhao Dianliang and has approximately 5,000 soldiers, including an engineering regiment of approximately 1,000 soldiers, all of whom are workers from ordnance factories. It is currently stationed in the Fushun and Liaoning areas. Recently, it destroyed the Northeast General Power Plant under Japanese jurisdiction, and the Shenyang area has become a world of darkness. It is hoped that patriotic people from all walks of life will do their best to provide assistance in terms of spiritual and material support in order to resist to the end. The troops plan to concentrate in Kailu, advance towards the Datong Line, and unite with the Volunteer Army in western Liaoning, using the Haicheng, Fushun, and Haicheng units as internal support and the cavalry group as the main combat force.

Mr. Huang Tingyu is currently the deputy commander of the army. According to him, the improvement of the Flying Arrow is currently under active research. In the future, it is planned to have the same trajectory as the mortar. The lower part will be equipped with an elevator, the same as the anti-aircraft gun's elevator, and the middle part will be equipped with an angle machine, so that shooting at aircraft will be more accurate. The explosives used are purely self-made and do not use foreign goods. Once sufficient economic resources are available, manufacturing can begin and be distributed to various armies in the Northeast.

Aviation Construction Association Seeks Cooperation Talent 122

The China Aviation Construction Association recently stated that aviation construction depends on talent. However, in view of the fact that domestic aviation professionals are already as rare as morning stars, and when they gather together, they often suffer from a lack of available people, while those who have talent and are waiting for employment often suffer from not knowing where to turn. Therefore, the Association recently plans to investigate talent who have close relationships with the aviation industry from all parties, regardless of whether they are current or former pilots, mechanics, engineers, repair craftsmen, and various experts in aviation, to register them in detail so that they can be employed as much as possible when various constructions of the Association begin. At other times, they can be introduced to other places to exchange information and knowledge, and be the first step in connecting and concentrating aviation talent across the country. It is heard that applicants should fill in (1) name, (2) native place, (3) age, (4) address, (5) qualifications, (6) experience (including what work they have undertaken), where, when, and how much salary, etc.

Public Bus Strike Workers Scheduled to Petition the Municipal Government Today 123

▲ The Crowd Was Outraged at Yesterday's General Assembly

▲ Traffic on Various Roads Continues to Be Disrupted

Since the British-owned public bus workers went on strike, a stalemate has been formed due to the company's tough attitude and the recruitment of new workers. The workers held another general assembly yesterday and decided to petition the Municipal Government this morning. If there is no solution, they will resolutely use force to prevent traffic. The details are as follows:

▲ Workers' General Assembly: At 2:00 p.m. yesterday, all the workers held another general assembly at a certain place on Avenue des Soeurs, with more than 200 people attending. The crowd was very outraged. The presidium reported on the progress of the contact with the Ratepayers Association and resolved: (1) All workers will wear uniforms and walk to the Municipal Government to petition on the morning of the 19th; (2) A general demonstration will be held on a scheduled date; (3) All passengers are respectfully advised not to take the public bus to avoid being affected; (4) Resolutely use force to deal with new ticket sellers.

▲ Presentation to the Municipal Government: The strike committee submitted a report to the Municipal Government, stating that the workers, under the oppression of imperialism, could no longer bear it. After spontaneously going on strike, repeated attempts to negotiate by sending representatives were refused. The workers are in a dilemma and their livelihoods are urgent. It is inevitable that disturbances will occur to public security. A request has been made to the Shanghai Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau to negotiate with the company, but it has not been accepted at all, so that more than 300 workers and thousands of family members have no way to rely on their lives. A general assembly was held yesterday morning, and it was decided that all the workers would petition the government and designate Shi Baoshan, Wang Xingmao, He Duanquan, and Zhang Bolin as worker representatives. They begged for sympathy for the workers' difficulties and the urgency of their livelihoods, and quickly sent officials to negotiate with the company, and it was necessary to decide on five temporary measures: (1) Immediately stop recruiting new workers; (2) Quickly restore the workers' original jobs; (3) Implement wage increases; (4) Wages during the strike period will be paid as usual; (5) No workers may be fired under any pretext. The above five items are the lowest demands of the workers. They implore the Governor to approve the acceptance in order to maintain the workers' livelihood and increase national prestige. They respectfully present with urgency and cannot wait for orders.

▲ Continued Disturbances: At 10:00 a.m., Route 1 public bus was driving near Avenue Haig and Route 9 was driving to Avenue Foch and other places, and striking workers threw hollowed-out watermelons filled with feces into the bus. For a time, the smell spread everywhere, and passengers suffered collateral damage. Therefore, there were few passengers on the buses in the afternoon, fearing that they would be innocently affected. When the Route 5 bus was driving on North Henan Road, it was surrounded by striking workers who beat a Russian ticket seller severely. Then Chinese police arrived, and the workers dispersed.

▲ Passenger Negotiations: At 10:00 a.m. yesterday, two passengers went to the Transport Office of the Headquarters of the Road Connaught Company to negotiate. According to them, they paid to take the bus, but they were thrown feces by the striking workers, which was harmful to health, and demanded compensation from the company. A certain employee of the company received them and said that the company no longer recognized the striking workers and had completely dismissed them, so the company was not responsible for anything. The passengers admitted that they were unlucky and left.

▲ Request for Assistance: The Strike Committee issued a declaration yesterday, requesting assistance from all sectors, saying that under the oppression of imperialism, they endured and served painfully, but were unreasonably dismissed. The workers' livelihoods are difficult, and the strike time may not be resolved for a while. They requested economic and material assistance from all sectors. The workers are very grateful.

Part of the Sanyou Factory Workers Have Been on Hunger Strike Since Yesterday 124

▲ Another Crying Appeal Group Formed to Appeal to Various Organizations

The shutdown dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Corporation's main factory in Yinxiang Port has been ongoing for over half a year without resolution. The workers have repeatedly appealed until their voices are hoarse. Consequently, they have organized a hunger strike group as a final plea. Starting yesterday, twenty-three members of the group have been on hunger strike to awaken the capitalists. Simultaneously, a crying appeal group has been formed to appeal to party and government organizations and various groups, requesting sympathy and assistance from all sectors. The details are as follows:

▲ Condition of the Hunger-Striking Workers: A portion of the workers, including Liu Yuanxing, Xie Ronggui, Shen Yucheng, Yang Xiutang, Mao Zhaocheng, Fan Yinchuan, Gao Jinshan, Yan Qilang, Gong Yushu, Zhang Zegang, Ding Qiaolang, He Mingzhang, Lu Shiying, Ma Jinchun, Sun Fanren, Zhang Ruitang, Wang Lizhong, Wang Chongzhi, Liu Yushan, Hong Jiaben, Hou Zhangyuan, Zhao Weiyin, and Qu Qifeng, totaling twenty-three individuals, after issuing a hunger strike declaration, have been on hunger strike since yesterday. They are all lying weakly in the dilapidated room of the factory's cool yarn section, in a miserable and pitiful state. Despite attempts by various parties to persuade them to eat, the workers are extremely resolute and refuse to be persuaded. From morning till night yesterday, they did not consume a single grain of rice or a drop of water. If the hunger strike continues, their lives are in grave danger. Furthermore, the hunger-striking worker Hong Jiaben, climbed the factory's water tower in the morning to express his determination, but was later persuaded to come down by security police officers.

▲ The Crying Appeal Group Appeals Separately: After a portion of the factory workers voluntarily went on hunger strike, the other workers who did not participate in the hunger strike organized a crying appeal group. They elected Xu Shimo, Zhang Daqi, Wang Chuncheng, Qin Changgeng, Ge Yuting, etc., as members of the group. Yesterday morning, they went to the Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Government, Social Affairs Bureau, Municipal Bureau of Commerce, Citizens' Union, Taxpayer Chinese Association, Lawyers' Association, and other government agencies and public organizations to cry out about the labor-management dispute and the suffering of workers who have lost their livelihoods. Now, some have gone on hunger strike, please provide assistance.

▲ Party and Government Dispatch Personnel to Investigate: After learning about the Sanyou workers' hunger strike and the factory fire, the party and government agencies dispatched Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Headquarters and Zhu Guilin from the Social Affairs Bureau to the Sanyou Industrial Corporation's main factory in Yinxiang Port and the Cotton Weaving Industry Union in the Seventh District and the Fourth Precinct in the Fifth District at 2 PM to investigate the truth and persuade the workers to eat. However, the hunger-striking workers remained silent throughout.

▲ Petition to the Municipal Government: Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the Sanyou Industrial Corporation's worker crying appeal group sent representatives Zhang Tingliang and Kuang Linchun to the Municipal Government in Fenglin to petition the Municipal Government to resolve the dispute. They were received by Wang Shao, director of the Audit Section. After the representatives described the workers' plight, Director Wang stated to the representatives that the Municipal Government had great sympathy for the Sanyou workers. Without the workers' urging, the Municipal Government was already preparing measures. Although the Social Affairs Bureau's mediation had broken down, it had not yet been reported to the Municipal Government. The Municipal Government would wait for the Social Affairs Bureau to propose resolution conditions and report back, after which the Municipal Government would adopt and decide on them, or submit them to the arbitration committee for arbitration through administrative action. The representatives expressed satisfaction and withdrew.

At the same time, we hope that your association will notify all members to attend when the time comes, etc. Accordingly, in addition to replying to the association to notify directly, we hereby inform your committee for your information, and we hope that you will attend when the time comes to jointly overcome the difficulties of the times. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce bows respectfully.

Representatives of Dismissed Employees of the E'an Tax Transportation Bureau Come to Shanghai 128

▲ Plead with the Audit General Office to Issue Dismissal Fees

Since the E'an Tax Transportation Bureau was merged into the E'an Audit Office, the employees, fearing unemployment, found life difficult and lacked travel expenses to return to their hometowns. They repeatedly pleaded with the new and old directors, and forwarded their request to the deployment and the Audit General Office, requesting approval to issue two months' dismissal fees. However, a month has passed and the superiors have not yet approved it. The employees are extremely anxious and have specially sent representatives Long Yuhuang and Yi Dade, etc., to Shanghai to personally plead with Zhu, the acting director of the Audit General Office, requesting prompt issuance. The representatives arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. Yesterday morning at 9 AM, they called on Acting Director Zhu. Acting Director Zhu immediately sent a section chief to meet with them. After the representatives stated their intentions, the section chief replied that half a month's dismissal fee would be issued and that the E'an Audit Office had been instructed to do so by telegram. Later, the representatives explained the employees' hardships and the special circumstances of E'an, and pointed out that Xiang'an, despite having no surplus, still issued one month's dismissal fee, while E'an, with a surplus, only issued half a month, which was unfair. They requested that Acting Director Zhu approve the issuance of two months' worth to show compassion. However, the section chief said that the telegram had already been sent and could not be changed easily. If there were reasons, the representatives could submit a request to increase the amount by following the precedent. The representatives then took their leave and prepared to draft an urgent telegram to present to the Audit General Office tomorrow.

The Book Industry Association Runs National Crisis Savings 129

▲ Extract One Thousandth of the Capital

▲ If You Buy Enemy Goods, You Will Be Fined According to the Amount

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously resolved at a members' meeting to organize national crisis savings. The detailed methods should be determined by each industry based on its own circumstances. The association received a report from the Book Industry Association stating that it had resolved to organize national crisis savings in four articles at the first executive committee meeting of the second session and reported it to the association. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that the methods formulated by the industry are thorough and commendable and should be approved for filing. It also replied that the handling situation should still be reported at any time for evaluation. The methods are recorded as follows: (1) In the first year, one-thousandth of the capital should be deposited by the member in the bank, and the passbook should be deposited in the association. If savings are still required in the second year, one-thousandth of the capital should be deposited again, and the same procedure should be followed. (2) The paper materials sealed last year will be unsealed by the association, and 5% of the original value will be used as national crisis savings (stored according to the first method) for use. However, products sold directly are still not allowed to be sold. (3) It is not allowed to purchase enemy goods in the future. If there is any violation, please report it to all sectors, and the association will send personnel to seal it up. In addition to confiscation, a fine will be imposed according to the original value (that is, a fine of a certain amount for each yuan of goods seized). Half of the fine will be used for national crisis savings, and half will be given to the person who reports it. (4) Those who do not comply with the above three methods shall be punished by (1) expulsion from membership, (2) no dealings with the same industry, and (3) announcement in the newspaper.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Resolves Not to Use Hunchun White Poplar for the Time Being 130

▲ Do Not Indirectly Open Up Profit Sources for the Japanese

▲ Use Yang Wood Unrelated to Japan Instead

Hunchun white poplar is one of the raw materials for matches. Since Liaoji was occupied by the tyrannical Japanese, the area has also been under Japanese influence. The extraction and transportation of timber must be handled by the Japanese and transported by Japanese ships. This matter was raised for discussion at the seventh standing committee meeting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. After detailed research, it was deemed that sales should be temporarily banned. The following is a record of the correspondence on this case:

▲ Letter from the Match Industry: The National Match Federation sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that it had previously learned from members' reports that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce had convened a discussion among match industry members in Shanghai, instructing them to use goods from other countries rather than domestic goods when purchasing match raw materials and wood for making stems, in order to implement the original intention of boycott. After hearing this, we were deeply impressed. It is now found that one type of wood used to make match stems is Hunchun poplar. There have been many imports recently. The price is about 40% lower per foot than Russian poplar. If it can be used, the cost per box of matches can be reduced by two yuan. However, Hunchun is currently under Japanese influence. The extraction and transportation of this wood must be handled by the Japanese and transported by Japanese merchant ships to reach Shanghai. In this situation, is it related to Japanese goods? If it is considered unrelated, we plan to notify our members to adopt it separately to reduce the cost of matches. This matter concerns the interests of our industry, so we dare to consult specifically and ask for a clear explanation for compliance.

▲ Reply from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: We received your letter on the 17th of this month, asking whether Hunchun white poplar, which is 40% cheaper per foot than Russian poplar, can be used. We have investigated and your letter also stated that Hunchun is currently under Japanese influence, and the extraction and transportation of this wood must be handled by the Japanese and transported by Japanese merchant ships to reach it. At present, the adoption and extraction of Hunchun white poplar indirectly means creating a source of profit for the Japanese. We can only endure the pain and switch to Yang wood unrelated to Japan. Although the price is higher, in order to implement the purpose of economic severance from Japan, we can only do so. We hope that your association will persuade fellow industries to follow suit.

▲ Electrical Machinery Silk Weaving Factory: The Shanghai Electrical Machinery Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association recently issued an urgent notice yesterday because of reports that unscrupulous merchants were selling inferior yarns, changing trademarks, and posing as domestic goods, which could cause confusion and deception for fellow industries when purchasing raw materials. The notice states that since the Wanbaoshan incident last year, the association followed all sectors in striving for economic severance from Japan, and at the same time obeyed the orders of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to establish a Japanese Goods Inspection Group to handle the sealing of Japanese goods in the same industry and to pay attention to weaving raw materials and all kinds of machinery supplies. All goods that were previously reliant on Japanese goods were replaced and eliminated, so that fellow industries expressed determination, promoted domestic goods, and persisted to the end without the slightest slack. To this day, the sealed Japanese goods have never been moved at all. Although this is the natural responsibility of merchants, it is also to save the dying situation in the nick of time. All the above resolutions were recorded and sent to you, and we trust you have reviewed them. Unexpectedly, the first and twenty-eighth of this year were again oppressed by the imperialists. Unfortunately, the suffering of our fellow industries was even more tragic. The war zone of Zhabei Hongkou has always been the area where our silk factories are concentrated. Once it was brutally trampled, it suffered infinite sacrifices. The cruel impression given must have been extremely profound. After the pain of our fellow industries, they must be united in hatred and determined to resist for a long time. Therefore, the association now reiterates its previous proposal and automatically expresses its determination. Regardless of any sacrifices, it will never buy inferior goods again, and will persist to the end, adhering to the original intention of patriotism and encouraging each other to jointly save the dying situation. In this way, on the one hand, we will do our best to adopt domestic goods to promote them, and on the other hand, we can revitalize the industry and promote the various fabrics of our fellow industries as much as possible. All sectors of society are full of patriots and will definitely recognize the domestic goods of this factory and be happy to adopt them. However, recently there have been reports that some unscrupulous merchants are selling inferior yarns, changing trademarks, and posing as domestic goods. If you are not careful, you will be deceived. Therefore, please pay extra attention when buying raw materials. Fortunately, do not be greedy for cheapness. You should first observe the source of the goods to see if it is reliable, and check the personality of the person in charge to see if he is honest, and then you can make the deal. Otherwise, if there are those who are willing to break the rules and collude with unscrupulous merchants regardless of the overall situation, once it is discovered and confirmed, the association will severely punish them and immediately expel them from membership, and the people of the country will jointly abandon them. This matter concerns the survival of the country and the life and death of the nation. Promoting domestic goods is our commercial responsibility. Please pay attention to it and do not regard it as a mere formality.

▲ Hat Shop Industry: The Hat Shop Industry Association recently resolved at an executive committee meeting to send a letter to persuade fellow industries to adhere to their original intentions and reject enemy goods. Local News 2

How Sad, the Motherless Child! 134

▲ Can't Eat Enough, Can't Keep Warm

▲ The Biological Father Flatters His Bed Partner to Win Her Favor

▲ Used a Thick Iron Chain to Lock Him Up in the Loft

▲ Imprisoned for Two Years, Feet as Soft as Cotton

丨Fortunately, a Righteous Person Reported It丨

丨The Police Have Filed a Public Prosecution丨

Dong Renbao, a native of Ningbo, 38 years old, used to be a tailor and newspaper vendor. He and his second wife, Ms. Chen from Xiangshan, Guangdong, rented a room behind the Wanshouchang Coffin Shop at No. 170-172 Meibai Road. Dong's first wife passed away eight years ago, leaving behind a son, Genfu, who is now only 13 years old. Four years ago, Dong began to live with Ms. Chen as his second wife. At that time, she was in her early twenties. After one year of marriage, she gave birth to a daughter, whom she loved dearly. However, she regarded Dong's son from his previous wife as a thorn in her side, not giving him enough to eat or keep warm. Although Min Zilu wore clothes made of reeds, Genfu could not even get that. The ignorant child could not bear the suffering of cold and hunger, so whenever he saw his father,

he would tug at his clothes and cry. Dong Renbao was unusually afraid of his wife. Whenever he heard her roar like a lion, he would obey her every word. He only knew how to win the favor of his bed partner and completely abandoned his own son, allowing her to abuse him. The child often did not get enough to eat, so he secretly took things and exchanged them for money to buy food to satisfy his hunger. The long-tongued woman took the opportunity to slander him, accusing Genfu of stealing and forcing her husband to use cruel methods to strictly discipline him. Dong Renbao then used an extremely

thick iron chain to lock his son in the loft of the coffin shop, giving him only two bowls of coarse rice a day to barely sustain his life. The neighbors on the left and right all knew about this, but because they feared Ms. Chen's ferocity, they all adopted the attitude of sweeping the snow from their own doorsteps and did not dare to speak out or offer a helping hand. As a result, Genfu has been imprisoned for two years. Now, someone has spoken out righteously,

revealing the dark secret. The New Zhabei Police Station in charge of the area dispatched Chinese detectives Ding Huaguo and Zhang Gendi, together with Western detective Aiwen Si, to the coffin shop the day before yesterday to arrest Dong and Ms. Chen. They then went up to the loft and saw Genfu huddled in a dark corner, unable to be pulled up. Shining a light on him, they realized that his left thigh was chained

to a huge piece of wood and locked. The detectives asked Dong for the key. Dong took it from his pocket and gave it to them. Only then were they able to open the lock. However, the child remained curled up. When asked why he could not stand up, he said that both his feet were as soft as cotton, and tears streamed down his face as he spoke. The detectives carried him downstairs. Under the bright sunlight, he looked even more pale and emaciated. His black shirt and pants were filthy, and his feet were bare.

Those who saw him were all saddened and said that his parents were extremely cruel. Later, the Chinese and Western detectives took him to the police station. In addition to detaining Dong and Ms. Chen separately, they sent Genfu to Renji Hospital. The doctor examined him and found that the muscles in the child's feet and legs had lost their ability to move. Whether he would be able to walk again would not be determined until three months later. Yesterday morning, the police sent Dong and his wife to the First Special District District Court, and Genfu was still carried to the court by the detectives and sat on the floor. Later, Judge Wu Tingqi questioned him. First, the police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated

that the police accused the defendants of (1) violating Article 294 of the Criminal Law for causing injury, (2) violating Article 310 of the Criminal Law for abandonment, and (3) violating Article 316 of the Criminal Law for obstructing freedom. He then described the situation of solving the case. Next, Western detective Aiwen Si reported the investigation and the situation of arresting the defendants. Judge Wu immediately questioned Genfu. According to his confession, his biological mother had died, Ms. Chen was his stepmother, he had been

locked up for two years, and he was given two bowls of rice a day. He looked very depressed and had none of the liveliness of a child. From the judge down, everyone felt compassion for him. Then, Dong Renbao and Ms. Chen were questioned. Both admitted to locking up their son, but claimed that it was because he had been stealing things and had not repented despite repeated warnings, so they had done this, and that they had only locked him up in February of last year. Judge Wu verified the confession and angrily said to Dong and Ms. Chen, "Do you have children? Would you also shackle your own children?" He then ordered the police to carry the child to the forensic room. After the forensic doctor examined him, he was ordered to be sent to the Women and Children Relief Association for temporary stay. The defendants were remanded in custody and the hearing was rescheduled for August 23.

▲ Regarding the case of insulting members of the association

The Shanghai Press Association yesterday sent a letter to Chen Xinghan, director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway bureaus, which stated: "Dear Sir, we have received reports from members Xu Shen and Wu Dong stating that on the 6th of this month, President Wang arrived in Shanghai from Beijing by special train. As reporters, concerned with our professional responsibilities, we rushed to the Maigen Road and Zhenru locations to conduct interviews. A New Wireless Radio Broadcasting Station Established in the French Concession 136

▲ Broadcasting Begins Today

The Continental Daily reports that a new wireless radio broadcasting station has been established in the French Concession, named F.F.Z. It will begin broadcasting tomorrow (the 19th). Its broadcasting studio is located at 149 Avenue Joffre, with a wavelength of 224 meters and a power of 250 watts. The radio waves can reach 1,840 kilometers. The station's origin came about because after the Shanghai war broke out in February this spring, many French soldiers in Shanghai did not understand the English broadcasting programs and felt quite lonely. Therefore, a small French-language broadcasting station was established. Later, the results were quite satisfactory. Famous overseas Chinese businessmen in the French Concession then took over the station. Anyone wishing to contact the station can call 80567 to reach the broadcasting studio.

July Construction Report from the Municipal Public Works Bureau 140

▲ Zhabei's Proportion Has Returned to Its Original Position

According to the Public Works Bureau's report on the general construction situation in the city for July, 244 construction permits were issued for the entire month, excluding rural housing, covering a total area of approximately 43,000 square meters, with an estimated value of over 1.38 million yuan. Compared to the previous month, the area increased by over 7,000 square meters and the estimated value increased by over 410,000 yuan. Comparing the districts, Zhabei has recovered its original position, with both area and estimated value ranking first. In addition, 237 repair permits, 126 miscellaneous permits, and 15 demolition permits were issued, covering an area of over 7,000 square meters. Comparing the districts, South Shanghai had the most, followed by Zhabei. There were 220 corrective actions, one-sixth more than the previous month, mostly due to non-compliant construction. Zhabei district accounted for more than half.

Public Concession Health Conditions in July 141

The report of the Health Officer of the Municipal Council for the month of July states: The death rate for foreigners this month was 17.87 per thousand, and the death rate for Chinese was 12.72. However, the number of Chinese may not be entirely accurate. Pneumonia was the most common cause of death among foreigners, while tuberculosis was the most common cause of death among Chinese, followed by cholera.

Cholera had reached its peak near the end of July. The infection rate among foreigners was 0.61 per thousand, and among Chinese was 0.99 per thousand. However, many of these cases could not be definitively identified as cholera. The arrival of melons on the market coincided with the peak of the epidemic. However, according to recent research by the Health Department and the United States, melons are not suitable for transmitting cholera bacteria. Their relationship with cholera is probably due to their chemical composition and the effect on digestion. In summary, the Health Department advises people to immerse fruits in boiling water before eating them. Residents should adopt this method, which is simple and easy to implement. Even if the water source is clean, it should be boiled before drinking. Filtration alone is not sufficient.

There were many cases of heatstroke in mid-July. The reason is probably that the early summer was quite cool, and then suddenly became very hot, leading to negligence. The best approach is to wear cool and suitable clothing, avoid exertion during the day, and not overeat or exercise. In this way, heatstroke can be avoided.

The pathological research laboratory examined 3,013 samples, of which 1,731 were for cholera examination. The number of examinations in the last two months was the highest on record. Among the examined items, there were 51 milk samples, 125 mosquito larvae samples, and several well water samples. No cholera bacteria were found in the well water, but several were quite polluted. In addition, the Pest Treatment Room treated 75 people this month.

The isolation hospital established by the Municipal Council admitted 80 cholera patients this month, 57 of whom were Chinese. The reason for the relatively small number of admissions compared to other hospitals is probably due to stricter procedures. Many of the staff in the epidemic prevention injection team were sick this month, which hindered the work considerably. However, more than 49,000 people were still injected, and the total number of people injected has reached 136,397. Patients in the tuberculosis hospital made little progress due to the hot weather.

Milk production decreased by 14% this month. Four cases of milk adulteration with water were discovered. The licenses of one grade A dairy farm were temporarily suspended, and one grade B dairy farm will be revoked. Four cases of private milk sales were prosecuted. Due to the heat, the number of slaughtered livestock decreased this month. Approximately 800 cattle were inspected. The Xinzha small vegetable market opened this month. The night inspection and sampling by the vegetable market team was very busy.

The cleaning team was busier due to the investigation of cholera, disinfection, well water medication, and management of vendors. The Municipal Council's outdoor swimming pool opened in July. The new water filter is better than the old one.
