A Counterfeit Coin Manufacturing Organization Uncovered on North Shaanxi Road 144

Detective Chen Daquan and Zheng Huaili of the Huishi Patrol discovered that someone had secretly set up a counterfeit coin manufacturing organization at No. 261 North Shaanxi Road to disrupt the financial system. They coordinated with Western detective Oumen and secretly went to the address at about 9 o'clock the night before last night, arrested Xiang Rongfa, a native of Shaoxing, and seized 90 counterfeit dollars, 1,129 counterfeit double dimes, 8 genuine foreign dollars, dozens of chemical bottles of various sizes, as well as account books, printing and sales waste water, wooden boxes, etc. All were taken to the patrol, and Xiang confessed that all the counterfeit coins were received from Dingyu Money Shop at No. 294 Jiujiang Road. The Chinese and Western detectives then went to Dingyu to search and seized 1,700 counterfeit double dimes and 52 counterfeit dollars on the spot. The shop clerk Geng Taikun, a native of Zhenjiang, was arrested and taken back to the patrol for detention. Yesterday morning, Xiang and Geng, along with the counterfeit coins, were sent to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special District Local Court. Wang Yaotang, the patrol's lawyer, immediately rose to detail the circumstances of the case, saying that after investigation by the patrol, it was found that the defendants manufactured counterfeit coins by first removing the silver surface of genuine silver dollars and mixing the middle with copper coins. The case still has accomplices who have not been apprehended, and the investigation procedures have not yet been completed. Therefore, the two defendants will not be prosecuted temporarily and request permission to detain them. He then presented the counterfeit coins to the court. Judge Wu Tingqi briefly questioned Xiang and Geng, and Xiang hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. Judge Wu ordered that the case be detained for seven days for further review.

The Sun Jingchen Inheritance Lawsuit Court Order Mediation 145

Sun Jingfu, a former comprador of the Peaceful Foreign Firm, whose alias was Jingchen, passed away last year, leaving behind a huge inheritance of several million yuan. The eldest daughter, Ji Zhang, who married into the Tao family in Ningbo, hired lawyer Wu Zhiping based on the legal provisions for married women to inherit property and filed a lawsuit in the civil court of the First Special District Court requesting an equal share of the inheritance. The case has been dragging on for months, with repeated postponements of the trial. As reported in previous issues, at 11:00 AM yesterday (August 18th), Judge Shen Hong resumed the inquiry in the tenth courtroom. The defendant hired lawyer Zhang Shizhao as his agent. The defendant himself did not attend. Zhang Shizhao stated first that the case was a family dispute and that the law should be combined with compassion. The plaintiff and defendant were both family members, and there was no matter that could not be discussed. He requested that the court order mediation outside the court or transfer the case directly to the mediation office for processing in accordance with the law. He then presented a written opinion, which was very detailed and comprehensive. Judge Shen immediately followed lawyer Zhang's statement and asked lawyer Wu, the agent of the plaintiff, what he thought. Lawyer Wu consulted with Tao Sun on the spot and replied that he was willing to accept, but requested that the issue of whether the property was indeed owned by Sun Jingchen or had been granted to his son Bin Xuan be resolved first before proceeding with the mediation. The judge then instructed that since it was a matter of feelings, there was no need to be bound by the law. Both parties should do their best to mediate outside the court. If mediation failed, the court would set a date for a trial in accordance with the law. His words were very sincere. The two parties then left the court in accordance with the instructions. This heated family lawsuit may have come to an end. The original manuscript of lawyer Zhang's opinion is found and is urgently published as follows:

Sun Zhu Lingxian being sued by Tao Sun Jizhang for division of property, agent lawyer Zhang Shizhao's additional opinion statement, law is inseparable from emotion, emotion can help law, I implore you to take both into account and instruct mediation matters, I, the lawyer, acting for Sun Zhu Lingxian being sued by Tao Sun Jizhang for division of inheritance, one side says that all the property was created by the father and should be distributed equally according to law, the other side says that the property was left by the late husband and should be inherited by the only son. As the saying goes, a common man is innocent, but he is guilty of possessing treasures. This is also true of the so-called inheritance in this case. This is a family matter, I can't help but sigh. Although the Sun family is a business family, they respect etiquette and teaching. When the old man was alive, he was dignified and elegant, and the whole family was harmonious. The family affairs were all arranged according to traditional customs and old habits, and there was no discord between parents, siblings, etc. All arrangements were made in advance. Sun Jingchen, around the age of 45 or 46, fearing that he might not recover from his illness, had disposed of all his property, mostly granting the business that should be inherited to his son Xu Xuan, and giving each of his two daughters a gift when they were married, and separately allocating a fixed amount of 6,500 yuan to benefit them. The eldest daughter, Xu Zhang, who was favored by her father, had a very generous dowry. Her husband's business was booming, and it was due to the assistance of her father-in-law. The 6,500 yuan that was allocated to Xu Zhang was used to generate more money and increase her wealth. The Tao family is now among the wealthy families in Siming. Who bestowed this wealth? Friends and relatives can all testify to this. The second daughter, Yi Zhang, has not yet been married. The sisters-in-law depend on each other and share their resources. The funds for her future dowry will be as generous as her sister's. The 6,500 yuan has also been separately reserved and can be withdrawn at any time. Even based on this, the old man has been planning for his two daughters, and it is definitely not that they have nothing. As for Bin Xuan, he unfortunately passed away five years ago, leaving behind three sons and one daughter. The eldest son is now only 18 years old, and the youngest is not yet 8 years old. The widow, Zhu, who is the defendant in this case, is raising her young children and carefully guarding her home. Considering the total amount of the inheritance, it is not easy to determine whether there is enough to cover the living expenses and future education and marriage expenses of the children. Furthermore, reducing it will lead to insufficient resources, while the income will be greatly reduced. The orphans and widows, who are inherently unfamiliar with making a living, have unexpectedly seen the Sun family go from being well-off to being in dire straits. The situation of Ji Zhang is the opposite. Her family is already wealthy, and her situation is even better. The master has become famous and established a business, and it is thriving. It is not necessary to count the wife's wealth. It is unreasonable to ask her to analyze every penny with the descendants of her deceased brother. It is no different from taking food from the hungry to add to the wealth of the rich. How can the deceased father and brother bear this? Yi Zhang, who lives in the inner chambers, is still a person who shares the same property and feels the same pain. She is even more concerned. She has no intention of seizing her brother's share, burdening her widowed sister-in-law, and monopolizing huge wealth to show off. This is the natural sympathy of human beings. It has been argued that the current law for married women to inherit property has only been established for a few years. Compared with the deeply rooted customary law, it is not difficult to ponder the kind of changes that are reflected in social psychology. The Sun family is a traditional family, and it is difficult to blame them for not understanding the new legal meaning. Sun Jingchen's arrangements for his children during his lifetime were made with a clear conscience. According to the law, the will can be freely disposed of in part. Now that the soil is not yet dry, the testator's intentions are completely erased. Is it reasonable to consider it in terms of human feelings? The spirit of reform is to make laws, and the wonderful use of law is to harmonize. If this provision is implemented without considering the actual social situation at that time and without balancing and weighing it, there will be the sigh of having a law that is useless and the danger of breaking the bounds. On the contrary, the original intention of legislation may also be violated. In this transitional era, a flexible approach that combines human feelings and the law is inevitable. According to Article 2 of the Civil Mediation Law, "Civil litigation cases may not be filed unless mediation has failed in the Civil Mediation Office. The parties may also request mediation for other civil litigation cases." The original intention of the national legal system is that all disputes between relatives should be settled with leniency and feelings rather than law, or even by bending the law to accommodate feelings. Law is the body, and emotion is the use. When emotion and law are combined, the Dao is greatly connected. This is the case in all countries with the rule of law in the world, and it is even more deeply rooted and indelible among the Chinese people who respect etiquette and righteousness. This case is originally a lawsuit for the division of property, but tracing back to the origin, it is still a dispute over kinship and human affairs. Although its legal nature does not involve compulsory mediation, the way of the king is based on human feelings, and feelings lead to law, and law is established according to feelings. It is appropriate to say that it should be included in the list of cases that can be requested for mediation. When this case was not yet in litigation, public relatives gathered and discussed many times. The plaintiff even proposed a plan, saying that the Sun family's property should be divided into four shares, with Bin Xuan's wife and children sharing two shares, and Ji Zhang and Yi Zhang each getting one share. It is not that the burdens of the deceased brother's family are heavier than the two sisters. Because of this extrajudicial proposal, the friendship is deeply appreciated. The evidence is there, and it is not difficult to inquire. Moreover, the younger sister's intention to preserve the orphans is even more advanced. According to her proposal, the father's entire property should be divided into eight shares: one for ancestor worship, one for Ji Zhang, one for Yi Zhang, one for Ling Xian (the defendant), one each for Wen Kui, Hong Yu, Wen Lan, and Wen Da. At that time, the written terms of the agreement were signed to show solemnity (the video is attached) and shown to relatives and friends, and all praised it. Apart from this, there were many more discussions on resolving the dispute, either through the testimony of the middleman or through the presence of a lawyer. This shows that the two parties in this case are not stubborn and unreasonable people. As members of the same family, there is no matter that cannot be discussed. Although the distance is far, it can be cut and honed. Reading the plaintiff's complaint, the upper part is based on various articles of the Civil Code, and the lower part requires "the right to jointly divide the inheritance with Bin Xuan's wife and children and Yi Zhang." Is the phrase "Bin Xuan's wife and children" a collective noun or a distributive noun? If it is a collective noun, it is consistent with the above-mentioned legal text. If it is a distributive noun, it is in line with the eight-part agreement with Yi Zhang. The language involves two ambiguities, and the benevolent and the wise see differently. This is probably the intention of the lawyer who drafted the complaint, which is particularly vague and uncertain, and implicitly opens up a path for long-term discussion. Furthermore, although the method of news reporting is in legal terms, it is not enough to be a model. As for inferring people's hearts and desires, it should be in the middle and not far from the truth. On the morning after the last court hearing, a news report in this city contained an account of the case, which included "requesting that Sun Zhu's children be allowed to divide equally" (the original newspaper is attached). The reporter did not understand the legal provisions and directly recorded the events. The fact that the reporter wrote so much about Sun Zhu's children and the fact that the original complaint cited the legal text of the first order are not very consistent but are not aware of it, probably meaning that the analysis must be done in this way to achieve fairness, otherwise, the number of inversions will be reversed, and a widow and four orphans will have concerns about insufficient resources. Our country's trial system does not adopt a jury. This kind of simple and honest public opinion cannot be incorporated into the judge's decision. The lawyer does not avoid elaborating, and the above-mentioned popular views on civil litigation such as this case are sufficient evidence to overturn and break. Try to ask a passerby, do you agree to burden the heavy and take more to survive, and not hurt the unburdened and take less? Or do you agree to the unburdened take more to be at ease, because it is very harmful to the burdened and take less? What is the answer? Even a child can easily predict. Based on this, where is the crux of this case? It is clear at a glance. Based on the above, only in accordance with the provisions of Article 370 of the Civil Procedure Law and Article 2 of the Civil Mediation Law, I request the court to instruct the two parties to mediate, or directly transfer it to the mediation office to proceed in accordance with the law. As for whether the mediation is conducted during the trial, or whether the plaintiff and defendant are instructed to elect a fair relative or friend to gather and discuss outside the court, it is all up to the presiding judge to weigh and decide. The lawyer is not in a position to make a request. If this is the case, the law will not feel that there is a narrow and difficult law to uphold, and the people will not see that there are feelings that are retained and not expressed. It is both fair and virtuous, and it can be said to be convenient for both. Sincerely, Shanghai First Special District Local Court.

The Press Visited the Kang Yuan Manufacturing Factory 146

At noon yesterday, Xiang Kangyuan, general manager of the Kang Yuan Canning Factory, invited the press to visit the factory. More than 20 people, including Zhang Zhuping, Wu Tingchen, Zhang Shutong, Chen Zehua, Jiang Hongjiao, Shen Danqing, Gong Zhongxian, Ling Qihan, Ma Yinliang, and Fan Jingwu, attended. Xiang Kangyuan led a tour of the entire factory and then took a seat for lunch. Xiang Kangyuan delivered a welcome speech and reported on the current situation of the factory. Next, Wang Zhixin, president of the New China Bank, reported on the reorganization and expansion plan, saying, "It is found that there are eight canning industries in this city. The Kang Yuan factory is the most impressive in terms of scale and equipment. In terms of business scope, the Kang Yuan factory is about 800,000 yuan per year, which is comparable to the total business volume of the other seven factories. Most of the large companies in the country that need canning are customers of the factory, including foreign companies such as Meifu, Asia, and Deshigu, and merchants in the Nanyang Islands also order from it because its pricing is lower than that of foreign manufacturers. It is also found that the demand for cans increases with the needs of social life. For example, the number of cigarette cans required is hundreds of thousands per day. The demand for other canned products such as gasoline, tea, milk, biscuits, and various candies and meat and vegetable foods is also increasing day by day. Therefore, there is no need to adopt competitive means from the same industry to enrich themselves by expanding and reorganizing. If the original plan is followed to use the original machinery and equipment or sporadic waste materials to manufacture accessories, then the business scope will definitely be more impressive. After being entrusted by the Kang Yuan factory to design the reorganization, this bank spent several months and obtained the assistance of many experts to conduct a detailed investigation and review of the content of the factory. The results are considered perfect and are willing to contribute the research results to the society so that the world can understand the actual situation of the Kang Yuan factory to prove that it is a good investment. It is hoped that this promising business will be assisted by strength and win glory for our country's industry. However, this move by this bank is still in its infancy in the country. We sincerely hope that all sectors of society will give guidance. If the promotion of this bank receives a response from the society, then what is beneficial will not only be the Kang Yuan factory alone." Finally, Zhang Zhuping gave a speech, saying, "The rise and fall of a factory depends on whether the management is effective. The Kang Yuan factory is known for its application of scientific management and has the reputation of a model factory. Observing the factory's strict work, the workers' diligence, and the meticulous organization, it is indeed rare. There are dormitories, schools, hospitals, sports fields, and other facilities related to employee benefits in the factory. It can be seen that the factory pays attention to the health and education of employees and other fundamental issues. In recent years, there have been many labor unrests, but this factory has not been affected, which is no coincidence. It is found that the larger the factory, the more difficult the management. Now the Kang Yuan factory has been in operation for ten years and has a good foundation. Gradual expansion will definitely be easier to succeed than a new creation. Now the organization is changed from a sole proprietorship to a company, gathering talents and assigning special responsibilities to cope with the expansion of the business, which can make the management more stringent. It is deeply hoped that the future development of this industry, which is related to the national economy and people's livelihood, will be immeasurable."

Fire at Wangjia Wharf 149

▲ Fire Broke Out in Wang Xiaoshan's Shop

▲ Spread to Four Neighboring Houses

Wang Xiaoshan, a 49-year-old Hubei native, had been running a bamboo wares workshop at the entrance of Jichang Lane, Xiangma Road, Wangjia Wharf, Nanshi. Recently, due to the end of summer, business had been slow, and his family resided in the overpass building in the same lane. He had fire insurance on his workshop for over 1,500 taels of silver. Yesterday around 11:00 AM, a fire suddenly broke out, the cause unknown, in the overpass building where Wang resided. The flames quickly spread, breaking through the roof. The Firefighters' Union immediately rang the alarm. Fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene with pump trucks, connecting hoses and spraying water. However, due to the extraordinary ferocity of the fire, the rescue efforts were quite challenging. In an instant, the fire spread to neighboring properties: No. 613, Xia Futai's used goods store; No. 611, Zheng Gongyi's palm fiber clothing store; No. 609, Yao Fuxing's leather shoe store; and No. 1621, Yuan Cheng's roasted goods store. Fortunately, the firefighters exerted their utmost effort in extinguishing the fire. After about an hour, the fire was finally put out. Besides the one overpass room of Wang Xiaoshan, four rooms of Xia Futai's used goods store, two levels of Yuan Cheng's roasted goods store, one building of Yao Fuxing's leather shoe store, and one building of Zheng Gongyi's palm fiber clothing store, a total of more than ten rooms, were all destroyed. However, Xia Futai had fire insurance for 5,000 taels of silver, and the bundled old cloth was not easily flammable, so it was not completely destroyed. Yuan Cheng's roasted goods store also had fire insurance for over 3,500 taels of silver, so the loss was relatively small. The two shops owned by Zheng Gongyi and Yao Fuxing did not have insurance, so their losses are immeasurable. When the fire was raging, the police officer from the area arrived and took Wang into the First Precinct, First Substation. After a preliminary examination by the substation chief, because Wang had a large amount of fire insurance and the cause of the fire was unknown, raising many suspicions, he was ordered to prepare a document to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for a thorough investigation.

A Great Work on Railway Transportation Business 151

Railway transportation is the central point of all railway undertakings, possessing a public nature and certain obligations. However, with China founding railways for more than fifty years, which have always been operated and managed by the state, many people regard it as an official agency. Railway personnel often forget their mission. Now, railway expert Dr. Jin Shixuan has served in the Ministry of Communications and the Beijing-Shanghai-Beining Railway for more than ten years. His knowledge and experience are extremely rich. Now, he discusses the various transportation businesses of the railway from an objective perspective, clarifying both theory and practice in great detail. The entire book is divided into four parts: Principles of Transportation, Freight Transportation, Passenger Transportation, and Connecting Transportation, totaling 470 pages. It also includes various passenger and freight transportation ticket formats. It is truly a book that every railway personnel in our country should read, a standard textbook for transportation universities and business colleges. Furthermore, merchants engaged in transshipment business, seeking improvement in transportation business and transportation economy, can also take it as a reference book. For those in the country who study railway issues, it is advisable to have a copy in hand. Each copy is 2.5 yuan. The general distribution office is the publishing department of Dagongbao in the French Concession, Tianjin, 30th Road. Wanyan Injury Medicine is Scheduled for Distribution 159

Wanyan Injury Medicine is a secret recipe passed down through generations from Master Shangkong of the Shaolin Temple in Henan, directly inherited by the famous late Ming boxer Xu Tianlong. It has been used for over 300 years and has cured more than tens of thousands of people. Famous Qing Dynasty doctors such as Wei Junping and Wang Zhaodan tried various methods to purchase the recipe at a high price. However, their descendants adhered to ancestral teachings and would not pass it on to outsiders even if it meant losing their fortune. Therefore, the world values it. This medicine specializes in treating falls and injuries, both new and old internal injuries. At most, five doses will cure it. For those with broken skin, regardless of the size of the wound, unconsciousness, or festering wound, wind entering the body, eyes crooked, hands and feet twitching, shaped like a bow, as long as there is a slight warmth in front of the heart, apply this medicine to the wound. If there is a lot of pus, wash it with warm tea to avoid the wind and then apply it. If there is no pus, no need to wash it. Also, take a packet with hot aged wine, or if not drinking, with boiling water. It can bring you back to life, but vomiting is difficult to treat. Or, for cutting the neck and throat, or knife wounds causing intestines to flow out, simply seal the mouth with fresh chicken skin and quickly take the medicine to heal. Now, Xu's residence at No. 42, Hengchang Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, is openly helping the world. It was originally intended to be given away for free, but it was expected that the demand would be overwhelming. On the 13th alone, a total of 837 packets were given away. There were also numerous requests for distribution. Therefore, it was temporarily decided to charge 20 cents per packet and give away a thick volume of Buddhist scriptures to limit the demand. All pharmacies and major tobacco and paper shops are selling it on consignment.

Free Talk

Two or One Branch Talk

The "Fragrant and Foul" Lawsuit 164

— Zhan Lu

The two lawsuits that have caused a sensation in society are those of Yun Huifang and Hu Lifu... Yun Huifang is a patriotic youth, and Hu Lifu is a traitor from Zhabei. The difference in their characters, one fragrant and one foul, can be measured in distance.

In terms of property, Hu Lifu is a member of the propertied class, while Yun Huifang is a poor young man... In terms of age, Hu Lifu has passed the age of fifty when one knows the decrees of heaven, while Yun Huifang is still a youth with unsettled blood... In terms of experience, Hu Lifu has considerable achievements in military and commercial circles, while Yun Huifang is a novice who cannot yet be said to have started a career. In terms of names, the two characters "Lifu" are so self-confident, with the great meaning of a weak man having ambition. The two characters "Huifang" seem like a woman, which is very different from the meaning of "Lifu". In every respect, Hu Lifu is superior to Yun Huifang. The only difference is that one is a traitor, and the other is patriotic. Therefore, mentioning Yun Huifang is like entering a room of orchids, while mentioning Hu Lifu is like entering a stall of abalone.

Compatriots, you can wake up! Traitorous life is certainly not a business strategy... Having a lot of property is useless, being old is useless, having experience is useless, having a good name is useless. The facts tell me that the power of social sanction is very great. Everyone wants to lift Yun Huifang to the thirty-third heaven, and everyone wants to lower Hu Lifu to the eighteenth level of hell.

Social sanction is based solely on personality, not on status. Moreover, Hu Lifu is only a member of the propertied class, and it is useless even if he becomes a noble official. But look, the illustrious and powerful Grand Tutor Qin Hui is infamous for ten thousand years, while the insignificant Palace Small School Shi Quan is famous for eternity! Compatriots, you can wake up!

The General with Different-Sized Eyes 165

— Bi Cheng

Those in history who are known for their appearance are not necessarily all true. Mostly, it is to exaggerate the words of sages and heroes, saying that they are different from ordinary people. For example, Yao's eyebrows have eight colors, Shun's eyes have double pupils, and Yu's ears have three holes. All these are exaggerations. Later historians did not examine them and followed their shortcomings. For example, Xiang Yu also had double pupils, and Emperor Gao of Han had a prominent nose. Novelists, of course, added fuel to the fire. Some used historical books, and some created their own strange theories, such as hands hanging past the knees, eyes that can look back at the ears, phoenix eyes, silkworm eyebrows, leopard eyes, tiger beards, green eyes, purple beards, etc., almost countless. I don't know that this is all wrong. Sages and heroes are in their integrity and learning, not in their appearance. Having such strange appearances is to make them different. Ordinary people think that their appearance is ordinary, and they will not be able to strengthen their ambition and study, thinking that my appearance is only equal to ordinary people, how can I hope for virtuous and heroic careers? Those who gray the hearts of the people are the mistakes of ancient history. Mencius's book is righteous and strict. Chu Zi said, "The king sent him to see you, sir. Is there anything different from others?" Mencius said, "Why is it different from others? Yao and Shun are the same as others." It can be seen that eyebrows with eight colors and eyes with double pupils are not necessarily all true. Yue E Wang is called the General with Different-Sized Eyes. This is a real thing. One eye is big, and one eye is small. In ordinary terms, it is almost like uneven facial features. Common villagers often have this. Therefore, it is known that it is not an exaggeration of a virtuous hero to have this saying. The other day, I took my children to Hangzhou to visit the Ming Sheng Lake and Yue Temple. Seeing the statue of King E, I pointed it out and said, "Don't you see that the right eye is slightly smaller and the left eye is slightly larger?" They replied, "Yes." "Is it because the sculptor is not a master and has this shortcoming?" I said, "No. This must be because the gentry at that time were careful and instructed the sculptor to do it." It is said that after the Wind Wave Pavilion and the disaster, this bad news had not yet been spread to the palace, or Gaozong deliberately kept it secret. After a long time, Gaozong's mother and queen suddenly asked Gaozong, "Why haven't I seen the General with Different-Sized Eyes for a long time?" Gaozong was vague in his words to answer. Now the statue of King E is indeed with different-sized eyes. From this, it is known that the gentry at that time were careful and must have instructed the sculptor without any doubt. Also, according to the historical records, those with defects in appearance are almost all true records. For example, Wei Yongzhi had a hare lip. The doctor said it could be repaired. Fang Gan also had a hare lip. Yan

Stumbled 166

— Qing Ping

One day, I was wandering at a crossroads and accidentally stumbled after being hit by a vehicle. The people around me laughed.

May I ask: Who is happy to take care of this trivial matter? Naturally, the car ran away in a puff of smoke. Then a burst of frivolous laughter, the wandering threads of the frightened soul were grabbed from the coma. Yo! Knees, arms, covered in blood - dripping blood, damn it this pain is really unbearable, but the pain is yours to bear, who will comfort you? Even who will help you?

Remember this lesson. After a person falls, they have to rely on their own strength to get up. Relying on others is the most useless and will be disappointing. And, you must also recognize this point, this drama is painful, not joyful.

Shibo lacked teeth. Those who ridiculed him called him a proverb. The Northern History records that Yang Dayan's prestige spread far and wide. Between Jing, Si, Huai, and Mian, children who were crying were afraid of him, saying that Yang Dayan had arrived, and they would stop immediately. The History of the Five Dynasties records that Li Keyong had one eye squinted and was called the One-Eyed Dragon. The Spring and Autumn Gu Liang Biography says that Ji Sunxing's father was bald, Jin Queke was squint-eyed, Wei Sun Liangfu was lame, and Cao Gongzi was hunched. At the same time, they were engaged to Qi. Qi made the bald person drive the bald person, the squint-eyed person drive the squint-eyed person, the lame person drive the lame person, and the hunched person drive the hunched person. This is also a defect in appearance, ridiculed by neighboring countries. It is definitely a fact. It is different from the strange appearances of exaggerating virtuous heroes. Hangzhou West Lake has many tourists. For the statue of King Yue being with different-sized eyes, I am afraid that not everyone can distinguish it. Or they don't even know the story of King Yue being called the General with Different-Sized Eyes. Therefore, I record it randomly to tell later generations.

Random Talk in the Capital 167

— Zhu Jia

Since the signing of the Shanghai Incident Agreement, the population of the capital has increased sharply again. In the Qinhuai River, where singing and dancing are prevalent, every time the sun sets, waves of bees and butterflies, those who collect wine and seek food, come and go in a bustling manner, and the road is blocked. In the tea houses where singing is clear, during this humid heat, they are full every night. The small food stalls nearby offer both cold and hot food. Unfortunately, the equipment is simple and cannot attract people. The more elegant arrangements are the Living Ice Room on Taiping Road and the Everyday Coffee Shop on Xinjiekou. There are countless others that arise from time to time.

The rolling watermelon with a single eye is a wonderful product for cooling off. Because of this year's high heat and sultry heat, people are competing to buy it. As a result, sales are booming. It is said that 3,000 loads can be sold a day. However, with a population of 600,000 in the capital, each watermelon averaging five pounds, only one watermelon can be obtained for every ten people. I am afraid that the hard-working compatriots who work hard all day will still not be able to enjoy it universally. Is something as low as a melon also thick for them and thin for us?

The Central Swimming Pool is next to the National Sports Field in Linggu Temple, which is far from the city. The equipment is magnificent and incomparably luxurious. Commentators say that it is becoming aristocratic because the round-trip fare and the cost of buying a ticket to enter the pool are beyond the economic reach of the average citizen. A few days before the opening, Wang Jingwei and his wife once went to the pond with Tieci and Zeng Zhongming early in the morning and entered the water together to enjoy their water life. It is said that Wang has quite a bit of interest in swimming.

The four major trunk roads of the capital are gradually being completed. Zhonghua Road reaches Yuhuatai in the south and is an important transportation route and one of the four major trunk roads. Since Mayor Shi took office, he has started demolition and bidding, with a deadline for completion. The contractors think that the daytime is too hot, and it is better to work at night. Most of the gas lamps are hung high and work late at night. For example, the pipe laying project has been completed. It is said that the Capital Construction Committee plans to establish trams to run on major trunk roads to facilitate traffic.

Five points of regret, it is sad to say. The most noteworthy thing is that after a large number of enemy goods were imported, they were sold out in an instant. If they are shipped to various places, they are also protected by warships and armed escorts. The plan is perfect. As the saying goes, easy come, easy go.

Recently, the national situation is in danger, which is very different from the past. All those with blood should be united against the enemy. Why are these people confused by profit and do not know how to repent? They are slaves to enemy goods, which is even worse than shunning them. It was not until the bombs of the Blood Soul Team were fired repeatedly that they heard of it and stopped. In this way, life is more important than money. Is it also the saying that you don't cry for your dad until you see the coffin?

▲ Enthusiastic people attract a lot of right and wrong: Recently, it was reported that Yun Huifang, a member of the Blood Soul除奸 Team in this port, was arrested for throwing bombs to warn 奸商. Even if he treads on the legal net, he will not care. The listeners were all moved by it, and all admired the young man's courage of self-sacrifice. The country will not perish, all relying on this. However, in the eyes of the average old and prudent person, they will say that enthusiastic people attract a lot of right and wrong.

Dixiangzhai Speaks

Kang Youwei and Liang Qichao (Part 1) 169

— Gan Yi

Kang Youwei and Liang Qichao were teacher and disciple. Kang Youwei became famous for the Wanmu Caotang (Ten Thousand Trees Cottage), and Liang Qichao was known for the Yinbing Shi (Ice-Drinking Studio). Both of their graves are covered in green grass. The world has already forgotten the location where Kang Youwei lectured at Wanmu Caotang, but Liang Qichao's "Collected Works of the Ice-Drinking Studio" are known to almost every household. Kang Youwei and Liang Qichao had different orientations and their scholarship was also different, but their names, Kang and Liang, were linked together starting from the Reform Movement of 1898. Kang Youwei's original name was Zu Yi, with the courtesy names Changsu and Gengsheng, and another courtesy name, Gengshen. He adopted the meaning of Zixing's "Youwei" (meaning "to do" or "to act") and changed his name to Youwei. As for his courtesy name, he likened himself to a "Su Wang" (uncrowned king), showing his long-standing and sincere devotion and worship. Some say that Youwei often boasted that he possessed the qualities of Confucius. This is another interpretation. He was from Nanhai, Guangdong. He was appointed as a secretary in the Ministry of Works after passing the imperial examination. At that time, the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895 had just ended. Li Hongzhang, alarmed by foreign troubles, urgently sought peace. Youwei did not agree. He submitted a memorial detailing the gains and losses, arguing that defeat in war was a common occurrence, but seeking peace would only deepen the nation's humiliation. His suggestion was not adopted. His colleagues worried about his safety, so he feigned illness and left his post. Three years later, Dalian was seized by Russia, and Jiaozhou was seized by Germany. People were talking about the dismemberment of China. His liver burned with righteous indignation, which manifested in his expression. He submitted a memorial requesting ways to reform and strengthen the country. The Grand Secretary Weng Tonghe, who was in charge of the university, believed that he had caused the loss of the war and national humiliation and was unpopular in public opinion. He was paying close attention to those who were knowledgeable about foreign affairs and wanted to enlist his help. Therefore, he strongly recommended Youwei, saying that he had great talent. Hu Shengchen said that Youwei's talent was ten times greater. Emperor Dezong secretly glanced at Tonghe and said with tears in his eyes, "Youwei inevitably speaks grandly and exaggerates, but his talent is not being recognized. This can be seen between the lines of his memorial." The Empress Dowager did not like him and had no way to bring him into a key position. Moreover, his qualifications were still too shallow, so it would have to be done slowly. Later, Xu Zhijing, the Vice Minister of the Ministry of Rites, also praised his talent. Emperor Dezong then summoned him for an audience and ordered him to work as a secretary in the Office of the General Management of Affairs of Various Countries. Youwei was very dissatisfied because the six gentlemen, Tan Sitong, Lin Xu, Yang Rui, Liu Guangdi, Yang Shenxiu, and Kang Guangren, who were known at the time, had all been given positions as senior officials in the capital and were participating in the new policies. Guangren was Youwei's younger brother, and his reputation was far below his brother's, which made things even more difficult. Emperor Dezong initially wanted to use Yuan Shikai's army to protect himself and gradually implement reforms. The six gentlemen, being young and holding key positions, advocated for rapid progress, using the analogy of cutting tangled hemp with a sharp knife. Sitong was impatient and saw nothing as difficult. He secretly discussed with Shikai about killing Ronglu, using troops to surround the Summer Palace, and expelling the Empress Dowager to allow Emperor Dezong to rule in person. Ronglu was trusted by the Empress Dowager. The Empress Dowager hated the Emperor and also disliked the reform. Shikai pretended to agree but secretly revealed their plan to Ronglu. Ronglu then knocked on the palace gate late at night. The Empress Dowager was startled. Ronglu knelt on the ground, weeping and explaining the situation in detail. The Empress Dowager gritted her teeth and said, "Strike first! That is your responsibility!" Ronglu humbly agreed and retreated. The gentlemen were all executed. Youwei had already gone to Shanghai on business. Upon hearing the news, he changed his clothes, hid on a Western ship, and escaped to Hong Kong. He traveled to Europe and America, wrote "Travels in Eleven Countries," and established the Baohuang Party (Protect the Emperor Party). He raised funds from overseas Chinese. It is rumored that his accumulated wealth was very large, but it is not known for certain. He returned after the national crisis. He once published a long telegram discussing current affairs and published the "Bu Ren" (Cannot Bear) magazine to advocate the theory of Great Harmony. He still harbored resentment towards Shikai and wrote articles criticizing his fallacies. In order to win over people's hearts, Shikai intended to offer him a position in the Qing History Office. Youwei strongly declined, saying that "If I were to compile the history of the Qing Dynasty, Shikai would be the chief culprit. I cannot remain silent. Shikai would not tolerate it. I should do nothing." When Zhang Xun proposed the restoration of the monarchy, he invited Youwei to meet in Xuzhou. Youwei traveled by Jinpu Railway, covering his face with a palm-leaf fan among the vendors and coolies to avoid being recognized. Huang Pei happened to summon Xun to discuss major plans. Youwei secretly told Xun, "Now is the time. Delay will lead to failure." Xun then made up his mind and led his troops north. Youwei went with him. On the day they arrived in the capital, nearly a thousand people greeted them at the railway station. Xun went to visit Huang Pei and hinted that he should resign. Huang Pei did not realize what was happening and ordered Li Jingyi to reside in the Cabinet. Within three days, Xun helped the deposed Emperor Puyi ascend the throne, and the yellow dragon flag flew over the streets. People then realized that Xun had brought Youwei with him for this very purpose. A false decree appointed officials and granted Youwei the position of Deputy Director of the Bideyuan (Office for Assisting Virtue), which was a great disappointment to him. He publicly rebuked Xun for not understanding politics. After the failure, he fled to Shanghai. He wrote a letter to Xun saying, "We may never meet again." The meaning was clear. The government ordered his arrest, but he was spared due to the assistance of Qichao. While in Shanghai, he often held literary gatherings with Zhu Zumo, Shen Zengzhi, Zheng Su and others. Youwei said, "The best calligrapher of our time is Zeng Zhi, and the second best is me." From then on, he traveled extensively to the northwest frontier and then along the Yangtze River. He visited local officials everywhere, promoting culture. The officials admired his name and treated him generously. He gained some wealth and died in Jiaozhou by the sea. He was over seventy years old.

Sharp Rise in Gold Speculation 171

▲ Surpassing the 20 Taels Mark. Yesterday, the trend in gold speculation was sharp and the activity was lively. There were ups and downs throughout the day, but only a slight dip of five taels. Subsequently, it continued to rise by about nine taels, initially exceeding the 720 taels mark. This was because the silver market had fallen again and the exchange rate had also decreased. The resolve of traders was strong. The foreign exchange market was also stable, and the shorts made efforts to push forward, which further boosted the market. However, there were occasional fluctuations. At noon, news broke of a worsening situation, causing widespread panic. Selling pressure surged, and prices could not hold. Eventually, the 720 taels mark was broken, and the market turned flat, standing above 20 taels. The September contracts had dropped by one tael and seven or eight qian but later recovered to one tael and two or three qian, still posted by the shorts. For the October transactions, approximately 21,000 contracts were traded by various firms up to the previous day. The daily details are recorded as follows:

Later, Yuan Heng and others sold, and foreign exchange banks also sold, causing it to retreat to 21 taels. For the current month, sellers have prepared a large number of deliveries, estimated at over forty truckloads. Hardware Firms Offer Discounts to Clear Ordered Goods 186

The hardware market last spring saw excellent market conditions, leading various foreign firms to place large orders with hardware merchants, even doubling and tripling orders with manufacturers. As a result, the volume of goods arriving in the autumn and winter of last year was unprecedented in recent years. Meanwhile, the value of the shilling first plummeted and then surged, causing significant losses for importers. Consequently, they were hesitant to request the delivery of ordered goods. Later, the outbreak of war lasted for two or three months, further exacerbating the already difficult circumstances for foreign firms, making it impossible to urge customers to take delivery. Almost a year has passed, and to clear their inventory, the foreign firms are forced to offer discounts and urge customers to take delivery. Currently, British, American, German, and French merchants are voluntarily offering price reductions to expedite the delivery of goods. It is reported that dozens of foreign firms have been offering discounts to clear their inventories in recent days.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

Essays

On Speaking 191

— Buddha

Speaking is most difficult, first one must consider the person's position and character.

1. It is easy to speak from the position of an observer, and difficult to speak from the position of an authority.

2. It is easy to speak when out of power, because one is not responsible; it is difficult to speak when in power, because one must be responsible.

3. It is easy for an employer to speak to a servant, whether the words are appropriate or not; it is difficult for a servant to speak to an employer, appropriate words are acceptable, but inappropriate words may lead to dismissal.

4. It is easy to speak without taking responsibility, because the words are not binding and do not necessarily need to be acted upon; it is difficult to speak responsibly, because once spoken, one should be responsible for carrying them out.

5. It is easy to speak when right is on one's side, because one's righteousness strengthens one's confidence; it is difficult to speak when one is wrong, because it is hard to justify oneself.

6. It is difficult to speak with a calm mind and quiet breath, words must be considered carefully; it is easy to speak in anger, because one disregards everything.

7. It is easy to speak to barbarians, because they do not reason; it is difficult to speak to civilized people, one must speak according to reason.

8. It is easy to speak to those who understand reason, one can speak according to reason; it is difficult to speak to those who do not understand reason, because there is no logic to explain.

Literature and Art 192

Summer Swimming Miscellany 193

— Songzhai

The scorching sun hangs high in the sky, lotus flowers emerge from the water, undeterred by the heat, they still compete to show their beauty, radiantly red. (Sun Lotus)

People accustomed to enjoying lotus in the pond for cooling, only then realize the heat has passed. They envy the pure and clean nature of this flower, with its delicate and simple shadow reflecting on the moonlit waves. (Moon Lotus)

Standing tall and straight in the center of the water, gracefully fragrant and unrestrained, a gust of wind comes and rocks it unsteadily, suddenly turning and skimming across the silvery pond. (Wind Lotus)

From ancient times, a gentleman is known for his pure heart, untouched by dust or contamination. When is its color and fragrance best? When it holds cool dew, wet and deep. (Dew Lotus)

Science

The Manufacturing Method of Shell Buttons 194

— Zhuo Tao

The introduction of shell buttons to China is only about twenty years ago. In recent years, the demand for shell buttons has increased rapidly. Taking Shanghai as an example, the annual import of shell buttons from Japan is about 400,000 yuan, not to mention other countries. In recent years, there has been some attention, but the production is very small and the quality is poor, which is not enough to resist imports. There has been no accurate survey and statistics on the origin and amount of shell button raw materials in China, which gives us no way to investigate, but it is known that the production of bird shells in Tianjin, Hankou, Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and abalone in Shandong is quite abundant and of good quality. However, due to the underdeveloped shell button manufacturing industry, they are exclusively supplied to Japan as raw materials. It is heard that Japan's demand for shell button raw materials exceeds supply, and they often purchase from China and other parts of Southeast Asia. Their purchasing procedures are handled by Chinese merchants. It will not be difficult for us to purchase raw materials in the future. From this, it can be seen that the shell button manufacturing industry is very easy to develop and extremely beneficial to our country. Those who are ambitious should rise up and plan for it!

The manufacturing method of shell buttons varies depending on the type of raw material. However, the sequence of work is nothing more than: blank, grinding, edging, punching, bleaching, polishing, shining, and waxing. The following is a detailed description of each item in order:

(1) Blank: Blanking, commonly known as the first car, is the first step in shell button manufacturing, the embryonic form of the button shape. The machine is divided into power and foot-operated. The entire machine structure is rotary motion. Foot-operated is commonly used, with the right hand holding the drill bit up and down, and the left hand holding the shell, which is fixed on the receiving platform. Then, the foot steps on the rotation to move the entire machine, and at the same time, the drill bit is rotated down until it is drilled through. However, during blanking, the drill bit expands due to friction and heat, making it difficult to remove it temporarily, which not only makes the work difficult, but also easily loses the sharpness of the drill bit. Therefore, a water bucket must be attached to the machine to drip cold water for cooling.

(2) Polishing: The surface of the blank is mostly uneven, and without the procedure of grinding, it is very difficult for subsequent work. The machine is also divided into power and foot-operated, commonly known as the second car. The important parts are the flat circular emery wheel and the attached pusher. The blank is pushed by the pusher and pressed against the emery wheel, and the blank can be ground flat due to the rotation of the emery wheel.

(3) Edging: The style of the shell button varies depending on the edging. Place the flat blank into a cylindrical column, push the edging knife onto the blank surface, and rotate the cylindrical cutting tool to slowly edge the blank surface.

(4) Punching: The structure of the punching machine is very simple, similar to the edging machine, but its main shaft is four steel needles. The needle tip runs through a regular plate, and an iron frame with claws is attached to the front of the plate for placing the shell button. The pressing of the shell button is done with a flat iron strip, and it can be punched through in an instant after the foot is stepped on and rotated.

(5) Polishing: This stage of the project is to remove the sharp edges and corners and make the button surface smooth. Usually, a drum-shaped wooden bucket is used for rotation. The method is to first pour the shell buttons into the bucket, accounting for about two-thirds of the bucket, add clear water, two inches over the button surface, then add two handfuls of fine sand, and then close the bucket lid, and rotate continuously for several hours, or two days and nights, so that they rub against each other until they reach a smooth state.

(6) Bleaching: Bleaching relies on the power of chemicals to remove the dirt layer on the button surface and show the inherent luster of the shell button, which belongs to a chemical reaction. The ratio of chemical ingredients varies depending on the type of shell button. Here is a common example:

Water: 10 pounds. Sodium percarbonate: 5 spoons. Sulfuric acid: until the litmus paper turns red.

Water glass: until the litmus paper turns blue. Magnesium sulfate: about 10 spoons.

Place the shell button in the above-mentioned solution and keep it at 70-80 degrees with a gentle fire for one day and night to obtain it.

(7) Shining: Although the shell button manufacturing has gone through the above-mentioned procedures, the luster is still dull, and it must be reprocessed. Place the bleached shell button in a 4% solution mixed with hydrochloric acid and Farmali, etc., and rotate for 20-30 minutes. Take it out, wash it, boil it in boiling water again, and then put it in a shining bucket to strengthen the hydrochloric acid rotation. If a little ferric chloride is added, the luster will be better. After the rotation is complete, put it in clear water to cool it.

(8) Waxing: Waxing is another shining procedure after drying. The method is to first put the shining shell buttons into a cloth bag, add wax wood chips, and two people hold each other and shake back and forth for half an hour, then take them out and sieve them to separate them.

The manufacturing method of shell buttons is now complete. However, relying solely on academics without experience, the resulting products will definitely not be good. Therefore, rich experience is required to obtain good results. Academics and experience are complementary and go hand in hand.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

My Opinion on Improving Graves 195

— Zhu Yunzong

Ever since Guo Pu of the Jin Dynasty wrote a book on burial and created the theory of feng shui, ignorant people have regarded the burial of dead people's coffins as the key to the rise and fall, wealth and poverty, nobility and humbleness of a family. Since then, they have spared no effort in choosing tomb sites. Especially wealthy families, for a few coffins, specially hire famous geomancers to select places with good feng shui to build Yin houses, spending thousands or tens of thousands of dollars is not considered rare!

As a result, now when we walk into the fields, we see a grave every five steps and a tomb every ten steps. A good piece of farmland is often occupied by a "dirt mound." I think that if this continues, the harm will not be small!

What are the harms of graves? (1) Increase superstition: People believe in feng shui, value graves, and must spend a lot of effort on burying coffins. They want to seek happiness from the dark, and compete to believe in each other, and the evil habit of superstition is deepening! Moreover, with graves, they have to engage in ghost worship every year! (2) Waste money and time: Choosing a grave site requires hiring a geomancer, buying land, building a grave, and building a grave house, wasting a lot of money and time! (3) Reduce production: Farmland is the mother of produce. With more graves, many fields are occupied, and produce naturally decreases. Our country is based on agriculture, but agricultural produce is in short supply, relying on foreign goods. This is also one of the reasons!

The harm of graves is so great! Then we must hurry up and improve it!

Improvement measures: (1) The government shall order the existing graves to be excavated and reclaimed for cultivation. (2) The government shall delineate areas to establish public cemeteries and order the people to bury their coffins there. (3) Those who do not comply with the order shall be fined.

After abolishing private graves and implementing the public cemetery system, there are three benefits:

(1) Superstition can be eradicated.

(2) Money and time can be saved.

(3) Production can be increased.

My humble opinion is like this, what do you all think? Please participate in the discussion!

Pitiable

Internal Contradiction 196

— Ren

K graduated from high school. After he completed his graduation examination and was looking forward to receiving his diploma, he often proudly thought in his heart: With his qualifications and abilities, finding a job in society would definitely be welcomed everywhere. On his brow, there was often a shadow of joy and hope.

This is an old saying, but now it has become an unchanging definition: "Reality is contrary to desire: the greater the desire, the greater the disappointment." K stepped into the threshold of society, and he gradually admitted this sentence. But he did not show weakness, nor did he feel discouraged, he persisted. It is said that recently he has been introduced to work in a certain organization doing desk work. I was happy for him and was about to write him a letter of congratulations when I unexpectedly received his letter first. The letter was written like this, and in his handwriting, there was a lot of anger and bitterness.

Dear friend;

Without a job, looking for a job, no matter what job, I am willing to do it; having got a job, but unable to do it satisfactorily

Page 20

. This internal contradiction, young people have generally deeply felt the pain. The so-called mature and prudent elders, they will put on an iron face and scold, "Young people are absolutely unreliable, they are fickle and change their minds, where do they understand the spirit of service?......" However, I think, are young people not people? Young people should not be an exception to want to live! Friend! This mechanical and absolutely uninteresting work is the graveyard of young people! Rather than being stuck in the graveyard, wouldn't it be more sacred to sell my strength?

Perhaps you will advise me to be quieter and wait, "wait for the arrival of opportunity." But, friend, what a vague noun this "waiting" is! And "opportunity" and "arrival" are even more words to deceive the weak! However, I know clearly that this is vague, this is deception, but, what can I do to open it?

"Weak young man, who told you to run into this cruel and absolutely inhuman so-called human society? Since you are here, why not be brave and fight your enemies, attack, and get your food? Who is to blame for this?" When I was depressed and helpless, a mass of pitch-black things rolled in front of me, making a ghost face and also like a serious general, mocking and encouraging me. Friend, I have never wanted to extricate myself? Sometimes I even prepare to do it. However, what is the result? This unfortunate result will often make you imagine that you have escaped from this so-called society, this so-called human being, and gone alone to a deserted island—

A deserted island without a little bit of a trace of a cursed so-called creature and spirit, with disheveled hair and bare feet, naked, frantically running, jumping, rolling, roaring, shouting... it seems that if I die, everything will be clean...

Black Curtain

Recruiting Teachers 197

— Yong

Since Mr. K graduated from XX Normal School, he has not found a position yet... Yesterday, he took a piece of news from the classified ads of the newspaper and told me...

"Old C... Look, isn't this an opportunity? But I feel strange, to... the..." I took it over and looked at it, it wrote...

"This school is now planning to recruit several teachers. Those who are willing to apply, please go to Mr. X at No. X Lane X XX Road to contact, and need to pay a deposit of 20 yuan..."

After I read it, I felt inexplicable in my heart, and I couldn't help but suspect again. Finally, I said to Mr. K, "This is probably a trick... How can teachers require a deposit... I can't believe it. You should look for other opportunities. Don't be fooled. Sacrificing 20 yuan is a small matter. It's really not worth it to be a fool..." But Mr. K had been unemployed for a long time and was eager to find a job, so he didn't listen to me and went to apply.

Three days later, Mr. K came back dejectedly and said to me, "Old C, I regret not listening to you. Now I have been fooled. Not only can I not find a job, but I have also lost 20 yuan and become a big fool... Really unlucky, this 20 yuan was borrowed by my mother, I am really sorry for her," I persuaded him on the one hand and asked him about the situation on the other. He told me...

"I ran to Shanghai and found No. X Lane X XX Road. When I opened the door, it turned out to be a small kiosk. Sitting inside was a young man in his twenties wearing a suit. He asked me my intention and asked me to write three resumes and pay 20 yuan as a so-called teacher's deposit. The young man said... I will send you a letter in three days to let you know whether to hire you or not, because there are already more than 30 applicants, but there are only three positions. If you are not qualified, the deposit can be returned..." So I came back and waited at home for three days. There was no notification, so I thought I was not qualified, so I went to Shanghai to get back the deposit. Unexpectedly, when I got there, the door was also closed, and the person was no longer there. A notice for rent was posted on the door. At that time, I realized that I had been deceived, but it was too late..."

After listening to his words, I felt quite unfair in my heart, but what can I do? I had to comfort him, "One more failure, one more experience."

Bulletin Board

Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court 198

▲ Criminal Judgment: Gu Zhongmin and others were sued for encroachment (Main Text) The original judgment regarding the part of the crime and punishment is revoked, and Gu Zhongmin is found not guilty. ▲ Sun Chunji was suspected of buying stolen goods (Main Text) The original judgment regarding Sun Chunji is revoked, and Sun Chunji is found not guilty. ▲ Ge Jinrong returned to the robbery case (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. ▲ Zhou Baozhi and the defendant Tang Zixiang sued Tang Zixiang for false accusation (Main Text) The original judgment is revoked and the case is returned to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court for retrial.

▲ Civil Judgment: Wang Maomao and Wang Xiaogou sued for confirmation of the removal of the fence on the highway (Main Text) The above text is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. ▲ Mai Houlin and Mai Houchu sued for guardianship of children (Main Text) The original judgment is changed, except for the part that does not allow the appellant to take back his children. The appellee shall send the two parties' daughter, Iro, to the appellant's place to see her by a nanny twice a week. The appellant's remaining and other claims are rejected. The litigation costs of the first and second instances shall be borne by both parties (above August 18).

▲ Civil Ruling: The original ruling to dismiss the appeal and apply for restoration of the original state is revoked in the case of Yuan Chengji and other 59 households suing Changli Company for payment of rent and relocation of houses. The case is returned to the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court for retrial. ▲ In the case of Zhou Hoshu and Shi Shiquan suing for payment of goods, the appeal is rejected. The third-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲ Public Announcement Service: In the case of Wang Hangsu and others suing Xue Jialai Yangxing for commission, it was found that Xue Jialai's original address is unknown, and a summons cannot be delivered. Therefore, a public announcement service is made. It is hereby notified to the appellee Xue Jialai Yangxing (above August 18).
